**Methodologies and Machine Learning Techniques方法和机器学习技术**

1. **Graph Neural Networks (GNNs)图形神经网络 （GNN）**
    
    - **Application:** Modeling the structure and dynamics of deliberative discussions by capturing the relationships and interactions between participants.**应用：**通过捕捉参与者之间的关系和互动，对审议性讨论的结构和动态进行建模。
    - **Techniques:** Utilize Graph Convolutional Networks (GCNs) to aggregate information from neighboring nodes, enabling the analysis of influence patterns and information flow within the network.**技术：**利用图卷积网络 （GCN） 聚合来自相邻节点的信息，从而能够分析网络内的影响模式和信息流。
2. **Natural Language Processing (NLP)自然语言处理 （NLP）**
    
    - **Application:** Analyzing the content of deliberative discussions to identify themes, sentiments, and consensus points.**应用：**分析审议性讨论的内容，以确定主题、情绪和共识点。
    - **Techniques:** Implement transformer-based models like BERT for contextual understanding of text, and employ topic modeling algorithms such as Latent Dirichlet Allocation (LDA) to uncover underlying topics in discussions.**技术：**实施基于 transformer 的模型（如 BERT）来理解文本的上下文，并采用主题建模算法（如潜在狄利克雷分配 （LDA））来发现讨论中的潜在主题。
3. **Community Detection Algorithms社区检测算法**
    
    - **Application:** Identifying subgroups within deliberative networks that share common perspectives or interests.**应用：**识别审议网络中具有共同观点或利益的子群体。
    - **Techniques:** Apply algorithms like Louvain or Infomap to detect communities, facilitating targeted interventions to bridge divides and foster inclusivity.**技术：**应用 Louvain 或 Infomap 等算法来检测社区，促进有针对性的干预以弥合分歧并促进包容性。
4. **Temporal Network Analysis时态网络分析**
    
    - **Application:** Examining how deliberative processes evolve over time to understand the development of consensus or polarization.**应用：**研究审议过程如何随着时间的推移而演变，以了解共识或两极分化的发展。
    - **Techniques:** Use dynamic network analysis methods to track changes in network structure and participant interactions throughout the deliberation process.**技术：**使用动态网络分析方法跟踪整个审议过程中网络结构和参与者交互的变化。

**Applications of Graph-Based Models基于图的模型的应用**

1. **Contextual Preservation上下文保留**
    
    - **Objective:** Maintain the context of discussions to ensure that the evolution of ideas and arguments is accurately represented.**目的：**维护讨论的背景，以确保准确表示想法和论点的演变。
    - **Approach:** Utilize temporal graph models to capture the sequence and development of discussions, preserving the context in which statements are made and how they influence subsequent discourse.**方法：**利用时间图模型来捕获讨论的顺序和发展，保留发表声明的背景以及它们如何影响后续话语。
2. **Bridging-Based Recommendation Systems基于桥接的推荐系统**
    
    - **Objective:** Facilitate connections between participants with differing viewpoints to promote understanding and consensus-building.**目的：**促进具有不同观点的参与者之间的联系，以促进理解和建立共识。
    - **Approach:** Implement algorithms that identify 'bridging' nodes—participants who can connect disparate subgroups—and recommend interactions or information sharing between them to foster dialogue.**方法：**实施算法来识别“桥接”节点（可以连接不同子组的参与者），并推荐它们之间的交互或信息共享以促进对话。
3. **Visualization of Consensus Evolution共识演变的可视化**
    
    - **Objective:** Provide visual representations of how consensus forms and evolves during deliberation.**目的：**提供共识在审议过程中如何形成和发展的可视化表示。
    - **Approach:** Develop interactive graph visualizations that depict nodes (participants) and edges (interactions), highlighting the emergence of consensus clusters and the pathways through which agreement is reached.**方法：**开发交互式图形可视化，描绘节点（参与者）和边缘（交互），突出共识集群的出现和达成协议的途径。

**esearch Proposal: Leveraging Graph Theory for Enhancing Democratic Deliberation研究提案：利用图论加强民主审议**

**Introduction介绍**

In contemporary democratic societies, effective deliberation is crucial for informed decision-making and public trust. The rise of digital platforms has transformed public discourse, offering both opportunities and challenges. Graph Theory and Network Analysis (GTNA) provide robust frameworks to model and analyze these complex interactions. This research aims to explore how GTNA can enhance democratic deliberation by focusing on contextual preservation, bridging-based algorithms, and the evolution of opinions.在当代民主社会中，有效的审议对于明智的决策和公众信任至关重要。数字平台的兴起改变了公共话语，既带来了机遇，也带来了挑战。图论和网络分析 （GTNA） 提供了强大的框架来建模和分析这些复杂的交互。本研究旨在探索 GTNA 如何通过关注上下文保留、基于桥接的算法和观点的演变来增强民主审议。

**Background背景**

Previous studies have applied GTNA to understand social interactions and information dissemination. For instance, Centola and Baronchelli (2015) examined the emergence of social conventions through network structures. Similarly, Goel and Lee (2016) investigated small group interactions in large-scale decision-making processes. However, these studies often overlook the dynamic nature of opinion evolution and the role of bridging nodes in fostering consensus. Additionally, while models like the Friedkin-Johnsen model address opinion dynamics, they may not fully capture the complexities of real-world deliberative processes. There is a need for comprehensive models that integrate contextual preservation and bridging mechanisms to enhance democratic deliberation.以前的研究已应用 GTNA 来理解社交互动和信息传播。例如，Centola 和 Baronchelli （2015） 通过网络结构研究了社会习俗的出现。同样，Goel 和 Lee （2016） 研究了大规模决策过程中的小组互动。然而，这些研究往往忽视了观点演变的动态性质以及桥接节点在促进共识中的作用。此外，虽然像 Friedkin-Johnsen 模型这样的模型解决了意见动态问题，但它们可能无法完全捕捉到现实世界审议过程的复杂性。需要整合上下文保存和桥接机制的综合模型，以加强民主审议。

**Research Question研究问题**

How can Graph Theory and Network Analysis be utilized to improve democratic deliberation through contextual preservation, bridging-based algorithms, and modeling the evolution of opinions?如何利用图论和网络分析通过上下文保留、基于桥接的算法和对意见演变进行建模来改进民主审议？

**Methodology方法论**

This research will employ a mixed-methods approach:本研究将采用混合方法：

1. **Graph Construction:** Develop directed graphs representing deliberative processes, where nodes signify participants and edges denote interactions.**图形构建：**开发表示审议过程的有向图，其中节点表示参与者，边表示交互。
    
2. **Contextual Preservation:** Implement temporal graph models to maintain the sequence and context of discussions, ensuring that the evolution of ideas is accurately represented.**上下文保留：**实施时态图模型来维护讨论的顺序和上下文，确保准确表示想法的演变。
    
3. **Bridging-Based Algorithms:** Apply community detection algorithms, such as the Louvain method, to identify bridging nodes that connect disparate subgroups, facilitating information flow and consensus-building.**基于桥接的算法：**应用社区检测算法（如 Louvain 方法）来识别连接不同子组的桥接节点，从而促进信息流动和共识建立。
    
4. **Opinion Evolution Modeling:** Utilize agent-based modeling to simulate opinion dynamics, incorporating factors like influence, persuasion, and social reinforcement.**观点演变模型：**利用基于代理的建模来模拟意见动态，并结合影响力、说服力和社会强化等因素。
    
5. **Visualization:** Develop interactive visualizations to depict the evolution of opinions and the role of bridging nodes in real-time.**可视化：**开发交互式可视化效果，以实时描述观点的演变和桥接节点的作用。
    

**Data Availability数据可用性**

The study will utilize datasets from online deliberative platforms, such as Pol.is and Consul, which provide anonymized interaction logs. These datasets offer rich information on participant interactions, timestamps, and content, enabling comprehensive analysis.该研究将利用来自在线审议平台（例如 Pol.is 和 Consul）的数据集，这些平台提供匿名交互日志。这些数据集提供有关参与者交互、时间戳和内容的丰富信息，从而支持全面分析。

**Expected Challenges预期挑战**

Anticipated challenges include:预期的挑战包括：

- **Data Quality:** Ensuring the accuracy and completeness of interaction data.**数据质量：**确保交互数据的准确性和完整性。
    
- **Scalability:** Managing computational complexity in large-scale networks.**可扩展性：**管理大规模网络中的计算复杂性。
    
- **Ethical Considerations:** Maintaining participant anonymity and data privacy.**道德考虑：**保持参与者匿名和数据隐私。
    

**Next Steps后续步骤**

The research will proceed as follows:研究将按以下方式进行：

1. **Literature Review:** Conduct a comprehensive review of existing models and methodologies.**文献综述：**对现有模型和方法进行全面审查。
    
2. **Data Collection:** Gather and preprocess datasets from selected platforms.**数据采集：**从选定的平台收集和预处理数据集。
    
3. **Model Development:** Design and implement the proposed graph-based models.**模型开发：**设计并实现所提出的基于图的模型。
    
4. **Validation:** Test models using real-world data and refine based on findings.**验证：**使用真实数据测试模型并根据结果进行优化。
    
5. **Dissemination:** Publish results in academic journals and present at conferences.**传播：**在学术期刊上发表成果并在会议上发表演讲。

Recent research has advanced this field, addressing challenges such as the need for large datasets and the risk of overfitting. Below is a curated list of relevant papers published after 2020 that explore these themes:将图神经网络 （GNN） 集成到审议过程的研究中，为复杂、动态交互建模提供了一条有前途的途径。最近的研究推动了这一领域的发展，解决了对大型数据集的需求和过度拟合风险等挑战。以下是 2020 年后发表的探讨这些主题的相关论文的精选列表：

1. **"A Survey of Dynamic Graph Neural Networks"** (2024)**“动态图神经网络调查”** （2024）
    
    - _Abstract:_ This paper provides a comprehensive review of dynamic GNNs, focusing on models that capture temporal dependencies in evolving graphs. It discusses key techniques and categorizes models based on their incorporation of temporal information. _抽象：_本文对动态 GNN 进行了全面回顾，重点介绍了在不断发展的图中捕获时间依赖关系的模型。它讨论了关键技术，并根据模型对时态信息的结合对模型进行了分类。
        
        [arXiv](https://arxiv.org/abs/2404.18211?utm_source=chatgpt.com)
        
2. **"Cooperative Graph Neural Networks"** (2023)**“协作图神经网络”** （2023）
    
    - _Abstract:_ The authors propose a novel framework where each node in a GNN can choose different strategies (e.g., 'listen', 'broadcast') during message passing. This approach offers a more flexible and dynamic paradigm, potentially enhancing the modeling of deliberative processes. _抽象：_作者提出了一种新的框架，其中 GNN 中的每个节点都可以在消息传递过程中选择不同的策略（例如，“监听”、“广播”）。这种方法提供了一种更加灵活和动态的范式，可能会增强审议过程的建模。
        
        [arXiv](https://arxiv.org/abs/2310.01267?utm_source=chatgpt.com)
        
3. **"Rethinking Fair Graph Neural Networks from Re-balancing"** (2024)**“从重新平衡中重新思考公平图神经网络”（**2024 年）
    
    - _Abstract:_ This study introduces FairGB, a method to mitigate unfairness in GNNs through group balancing. It addresses distribution disparities between demographic groups, which is crucial for modeling equitable deliberative processes. _抽象：_本研究介绍了 FairGB，这是一种通过组平衡来减轻 GNN 中不公平的方法。它解决了人口群体之间的分布差异，这对于模拟公平的审议过程至关重要。

    - _Abstract:_ This comprehensive review covers various aspects of GNNs, including their application in modeling complex networks. It discusses challenges like overfitting and the need for large datasets, providing insights relevant to deliberative process modeling. _抽象：_这篇全面的综述涵盖了 GNN 的各个方面，包括它们在复杂网络建模中的应用。它讨论了过度拟合等挑战和对大型数据集的需求，提供了与审议过程建模相关的见解。

# A review of graph neural networks: concepts, architectures, techniques, challenges, datasets, applications, and future directions
In recent years, deep learning (DL) has been called the gold standard in machine learning (ML). It has also steadily evolved into the most widely used computational technique in ML, producing excellent results on various challenging cognitive tasks, sometimes even matching or outperforming human ability. One benefit of DL is its capacity to learn enormous amounts of data [[1](https://journalofbigdata.springeropen.com/articles/10.1186/s40537-023-00876-4#ref-CR1 "Pucci A, Gori M, Hagenbuchner M, Scarselli F, Tsoi AC. Investigation into the application of graph neural networks to large-scale recommender systems, infona.pl, no. 32, no 4, pp. 17–26, 2006.")]. GNN variations such as graph convolutional networks (GCNs), graph attention networks (GATs), and GraphSAGE have shown groundbreaking performance on various deep learning tasks in recent years [[2](https://journalofbigdata.springeropen.com/articles/10.1186/s40537-023-00876-4#ref-CR2 "Mahmud FB, Rayhan MM, Shuvo MH, Sadia I, Morol MK. A comparative analysis of Graph Neural Networks and commonly used machine learning algorithms on fake news detection, Proc. - 2022 7th Int. Conf. Data Sci. Mach. Learn. Appl. CDMA 2022, pp. 97–102, 2022.")].  
近年来，深度学习 （DL） 被称为机器学习 （ML） 的黄金标准。它还稳步发展成为 ML 中使用最广泛的计算技术，在各种具有挑战性的认知任务中产生出色的结果，有时甚至达到或超过人类的能力。深度学习的一个好处是它能够学习大量数据 [[1](https://journalofbigdata.springeropen.com/articles/10.1186/s40537-023-00876-4#ref-CR1 "Pucci A, Gori M, Hagenbuchner M, Scarselli F, Tsoi AC. Investigation into the application of graph neural networks to large-scale recommender systems, infona.pl, no. 32, no 4, pp. 17–26, 2006.")]。近年来，图卷积网络 （GCN）、图注意力网络 （GAT） 和 GraphSAGE 等 GNN 变体在各种深度学习任务中表现出突破性的性能 [[2](https://journalofbigdata.springeropen.com/articles/10.1186/s40537-023-00876-4#ref-CR2 "Mahmud FB, Rayhan MM, Shuvo MH, Sadia I, Morol MK. A comparative analysis of Graph Neural Networks and commonly used machine learning algorithms on fake news detection, Proc. - 2022 7th Int. Conf. Data Sci. Mach. Learn. Appl. CDMA 2022, pp. 97–102, 2022.")]。

# Message passing mechanism in graph neural network  
图神经网络中的消息传递机制

Graph symmetries are maintained using a GNN, an optimizable transformation on all graph properties (nodes, edges, and global context) (permutation invariances). Because a GNN does not alter the connectivity of the input graph, the output may be characterized using the same adjacency list and feature vector count as the input graph. However, the output graph has updated embeddings because the GNN modified each node, edge, and global-context representation.  
使用 GNN 维护图形对称性，GNN 是所有图形属性（节点、边和全局上下文）（排列不变性）的可优化变换。由于 GNN 不会改变输入图的连通性，因此可以使用与输入图相同的邻接列表和特征向量计数来表征输出。但是，输出图更新了嵌入，因为 GNN 修改了每个节点、边和全局上下文表示。

In Fig. [6](https://journalofbigdata.springeropen.com/articles/10.1186/s40537-023-00876-4#Fig6), circles are nodes, and empty boxes show aggregation of neighbor/adjacent nodes. The model aggregates messages from A's local graph neighbors (i.e., B, C, and D). In turn, the messages coming from neighbors are based on information aggregated from their respective neighborhoods, and so on. This visualization shows a two-layer version of a message-passing model. Notice that the computation graph of the GNN forms a tree structure by unfolding the neighborhood around the target node [[17](https://journalofbigdata.springeropen.com/articles/10.1186/s40537-023-00876-4#ref-CR17 "Fan W et al. Graph neural networks for social recommendation," in The world wide web conference, 2019, pp. 417–426.")]. Graph neural networks (GNNs) are neural models that capture the dependence of graphs via message passing between the nodes of graphs [[30](https://journalofbigdata.springeropen.com/articles/10.1186/s40537-023-00876-4#ref-CR30 "Zhou J, et al. Graph neural networks: a review of methods and applications. AI Open. 2020;1(January):57–81. 
https://doi.org/10.1016/j.aiopen.2021.01.001
.")].  
在图 .[6](https://journalofbigdata.springeropen.com/articles/10.1186/s40537-023-00876-4#Fig6)，圆圈是节点，空框显示邻居/相邻节点的聚合。该模型聚合来自 A 的本地图形邻居（即 B、C 和 D）的消息。反过来，来自邻域的消息基于从各自邻域聚合的信息，依此类推。此可视化效果显示了消息传递模型的两层版本。请注意，GNN 的计算图通过围绕目标节点展开邻域来形成树状结构 [[17](https://journalofbigdata.springeropen.com/articles/10.1186/s40537-023-00876-4#ref-CR17 "Fan W et al. Graph neural networks for social recommendation," in The world wide web conference, 2019, pp. 417–426.")]。图神经网络 （GNN） 是一种神经模型，它通过在图的节点之间传递消息来捕获图的依赖性 [[30](https://journalofbigdata.springeropen.com/articles/10.1186/s40537-023-00876-4#ref-CR30 "Zhou J, et al. Graph neural networks: a review of methods and applications. AI Open. 2020;1(January):57–81. https://doi.org/10.1016/j.aiopen.2021.01.001 .")]。

**Fig. 6 图 6**

[![figure 6](https://media.springernature.com/lw685/springer-static/image/art%3A10.1186%2Fs40537-023-00876-4/MediaObjects/40537_2023_876_Fig6_HTML.png)](https://journalofbigdata.springeropen.com/articles/10.1186/s40537-023-00876-4/figures/6)

How a single node aggregates messages from its adjacent neighbor nodes  
单个节点如何聚合来自其相邻邻接节点的消息

[Full size image 全尺寸图像](https://journalofbigdata.springeropen.com/articles/10.1186/s40537-023-00876-4/figures/6)

The message-passing mechanism of Graph Neural Networks is shown in Fig. [7](https://journalofbigdata.springeropen.com/articles/10.1186/s40537-023-00876-4#Fig7). In this, we take an input graph with a set of node features X ε Rd⇥|V| and Use this knowledge to produce node embeddings zu. However, we will also review how the GNN framework may embed subgraphs and whole graphs.  
图神经网络的消息传递机制如图 1 所示。[7](https://journalofbigdata.springeropen.com/articles/10.1186/s40537-023-00876-4#Fig7). 在本例中，我们采用一个包含一组节点特征 X ε Rd⇥|V|和利用这些知识生成节点嵌入 zu。但是，我们还将回顾 GNN 框架如何嵌入子图和整个图。


# Working of graph convolutional network  
图卷积网络的工作原理

A Graph Convolutional Network (GCN) is a type of neural network architecture designed for processing and analyzing graph-structured data. GCNs work by aggregating and propagating information through the nodes in a graph. GCN works with the following steps shown in Fig. [19](https://journalofbigdata.springeropen.com/articles/10.1186/s40537-023-00876-4#Fig19):  
图形卷积网络 （GCN） 是一种神经网络架构，旨在处理和分析图形结构数据。GCN 的工作原理是通过图形中的节点聚合和传播信息。GCN 的工作原理如下，如图 2 所示。[19](https://journalofbigdata.springeropen.com/articles/10.1186/s40537-023-00876-4#Fig19)：

1. 1)
    
    Initialization: 初始化：
    

**Fig. 19 图 19**

[![figure 19](https://media.springernature.com/lw685/springer-static/image/art%3A10.1186%2Fs40537-023-00876-4/MediaObjects/40537_2023_876_Fig19_HTML.png)](https://journalofbigdata.springeropen.com/articles/10.1186/s40537-023-00876-4/figures/19)

Working of GCN GCN 的工作原理

[Full size image 全尺寸图像](https://journalofbigdata.springeropen.com/articles/10.1186/s40537-023-00876-4/figures/19)

Each node in the graph is associated with a feature vector. Depending on the application, these feature vectors can represent various attributes or characteristics of the nodes. For example, in a social network, each node might represent a user, and the features could include user profile information.  
图中的每个节点都与一个特征向量相关联。根据应用程序，这些特征向量可以表示节点的各种属性或特征。例如，在社交网络中，每个节点可能代表一个用户，并且功能可以包含用户个人资料信息。

1. 2)
    
    Convolution Operation: 卷积操作：
    

The core of a GCN is the convolution operation, which is adapted from convolutional neural networks (CNNs). It aims to aggregate information from neighboring nodes. This is done by taking a weighted sum of the feature vectors of neighboring nodes. The graph's adjacency matrix determines the weights. The resulting aggregated information is a new feature vector for each node.  
GCN 的核心是卷积运算，它改编自卷积神经网络 （CNN）。它旨在聚合来自相邻节点的信息。这是通过对相邻节点的特征向量进行加权和来完成的。图形的邻接矩阵确定权重。生成的聚合信息是每个节点的新特征向量。

1. 3)
    
    Weighted Aggregation: 加权聚合：
    

The graph's adjacency matrix, typically after normalization, provides weights for the aggregation process. In this context, for a given node, the features of its neighboring nodes are scaled by the corresponding values within the adjacency matrix, and the outcomes are then accumulated. A precise mathematical elucidation of this aggregation step is described in "[Equation of GCN](https://journalofbigdata.springeropen.com/articles/10.1186/s40537-023-00876-4#Sec27)" section.  
图形的邻接矩阵（通常在规范化之后）为聚合过程提供权重。在这种情况下，对于给定的节点，其相邻节点的特征按邻接矩阵中的相应值进行缩放，然后累积结果。此聚合步骤的精确数学说明在 “[GCN 方程](https://journalofbigdata.springeropen.com/articles/10.1186/s40537-023-00876-4#Sec27)” 部分描述。

1. 4)
    
    Activation function and learning weights:  
    激活函数和学习权重：
    

The aggregated features are typically passed through an activation function (e.g., ReLU) to introduce non-linearity. The weight matrix W used in the aggregation step is learned during training. This learning process allows the GCN to adapt to the specific graph and task it is designed for.  
聚合特征通常通过激活函数（例如 ReLU）传递以引入非线性。聚合步骤中使用的权重矩阵 W 是在训练期间学习的。此学习过程使 GCN 能够适应其设计的特定图形和任务。

1. 5)
    
    Stacking Layers: 堆叠层：
    

GCNs are often used in multiple layers. This allows the network to capture more complex relationships and higher-level features in the graph. The output of one GCN layer becomes the input for the next, and this process is repeated for a predefined number of layers.  
GCN 通常用于多个层。这允许网络在图形中捕获更复杂的关系和更高级别的特征。一个 GCN 层的输出将成为下一个 GCN 层的输入，并且对预定义数量的层重复此过程。

1. 6)
    
    Task-Specific Output: 特定于任务的输出：
    

The final output of the GCN can be used for various graph-based tasks, such as node classification, link prediction, or graph classification, depending on the specific application.  
GCN 的最终输出可用于各种基于图形的任务，例如节点分类、链接预测或图形分类，具体取决于具体应用程序。

# Rethinking Fair Graph Neural Networks from Re-balancing

https://arxiv.org/pdf/2407.11624

https://arxiv.org/html/2407.11624v1


在图神经网络（GNN）强大的表示能力的驱动下，大量的GNN模型已广泛部署在许多实际应用中。然而，由于不同人口群体之间的分布差异，高风险决策系统的公平性越来越受到关注。尽管最近有很多致力于提高 GNN 公平性的工作并取得了相当大的成功，但它们都需要重大的架构更改或需要更多超参数调整的额外损失函数。令人惊讶的是，我们发现简单的重新平衡方法可以轻松匹配或超越现有的公平 GNN 方法。我们认为，不同人口群体之间的不平衡是不公平的重要根源，导致每个群体对参数更新的贡献不平衡。然而，这些简单的重新平衡方法在训练过程中有其自身的缺点。在本文中，我们提出了 FairGB，即通过重新平衡的公平图神经网络，它通过群体平衡来减轻 GNN 的不公平性。从技术上讲，FairGB 由两个模块组成：反事实节点混合和贡献对齐损失。首先，我们选择跨域和类间的反事实对，并对自我网络进行插值以生成新样本。在分析的指导下，我们可以通过因果视图揭示我们模型的去偏机制，并证明我们的策略可以使敏感属性在统计上独立于目标标签。其次，我们根据梯度重新权衡每组的贡献。通过将这两个模块结合起来，可以相互促进。 基准数据集的实验结果表明，我们的方法可以在效用和公平性指标方面取得最先进的结果。代码可在[https://github.com/ZhixunLEE/FairGB](https://github.com/ZhixunLEE/FairGB)获取。
![[Pasted image 20241124222019.png]]


![[截圖 2024-11-24 下午10.22.20.png]]

## 4.Experiments

In this section, we conduct extensive experiments to investigate the effectiveness of our proposed model, and aim to answer the following research questions?
    
    RQ1: Compared to other baselines, can FairGB achieve better performance _w.r.t._ utility and fairness?
    RQ2: How does each component affect the model performance?
    RQ3: What are the characteristics of the node features generated by FairGB compared to vanilla?
    RQ4: Can FairGB generalize well to different graph encoders?
    RQ5: How do hyper-parameters affect FairGB?


# Cooperative Graph Neural Networks
https://arxiv.org/html/2310.01267v2

https://github.com/Oliz888/CoGNN
```
@inproceedings{finkelshtein2023cooperative,
  title = "Cooperative Graph Neural Networks",
  author = "Ben Finkelshtein and Xingyue Huang and Michael Bronstein and {\.I}smail {\.I}lkan Ceylan",
  year = "2024",
  booktitle = "Proceedings of Forty-first International Conference on Machine Learning (ICML)",
  url = "https://arxiv.org/abs/2310.01267",
}
```


Graph neural networks are popular architectures for graph machine learning, based on iterative computation of node representations of an input graph through a series of invariant transformations. A large class of graph neural networks follow a standard message-passing paradigm: at every layer, each node state is updated based on an aggregate of messages from its neighborhood. In this work, we propose a novel framework for training graph neural networks, where every node is viewed as a _player_ that can choose to either ‘listen’, ‘broadcast’, ‘listen and broadcast’, or to ‘isolate’. The standard message propagation scheme can then be viewed as a special case of this framework where every node ‘listens and broadcasts’ to all neighbors. Our approach offers a more flexible and dynamic message-passing paradigm, where each node can determine its own strategy based on their state, effectively exploring the graph topology while learning. We provide a theoretical analysis of the new message-passing scheme which is further supported by an extensive empirical analysis on synthetic and real-world data.  
图神经网络是图机器学习的流行架构，基于通过一系列不变变换对输入图的节点表示进行迭代计算。一大类图神经网络遵循标准的消息传递范例：在每一层，每个节点状态都根据来自其邻居的消息聚合进行更新。在这项工作中，我们提出了一种用于训练图神经网络的新颖框架，其中每个节点都被视为可以选择“收听”、“广播”、“收听和广播”或“隔离”的_玩家_。标准消息传播方案可以被视为该框架的一个特例，其中每个节点都向所有邻居“监听和广播”。我们的方法提供了更灵活和动态的消息传递范例，其中每个节点都可以根据其状态确定自己的策略，在学习时有效地探索图拓扑。我们提供了对新消息传递方案的理论分析，并得到了对合成数据和现实世界数据的广泛实证分析的进一步支持

As established and emerging social groups splinter and gather together in online spaces, ‘othering’ proliferates.
