# An AI-Enhanced Solution for Large Scale Deliberation Mapping and Explainable Reasoning 
https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-031-30694-5_23?utm_source=chatgpt.com


State-of-the-art approaches attempt to address the following major challenges (Tang and Liao, [2019](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-031-30694-5_23?utm_source=chatgpt.com#ref-CR19 "Tang, M., Liao, H.: From conventional group decision making to large-scale group decision making: what are the challenges and how to meet them in big data era? A state-of-the-art survey. Omega 102141 (2019). 
https://doi.org/10.1016/j.omega.2019.102141")): _(i) reduction of the decision makers’ dimension:_ clustering analysis is the most widely used method so far, aiming to reduce the complexity and cost of the associated problems, as well as to identify common opinion patterns (e.g. clusters with similar opinions and a spokesman who represents each cluster); _(ii) weighting and aggregating decision information:_ the development of a reasonable method that considers the diverse characteristics of individuals and subgroups to determine weights is very crucial, making simple aggregation strategies such as arithmetic average or weighted average not appropriate; _(iii) management of participants’ behavior:_ existing studies often adopt a social network analysis perspective to investigate the consensus reaching process and the associated detection and elimination of conflicts among decision makers (Liu _et al._, [2019](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-031-30694-5_23?utm_source=chatgpt.com#ref-CR15 "Liu, B.S., Zhou, Q., Ding, R.X., Palomares, I., Herrera, F.: Large-scale group decision making model based on social network analysis: trust relationship-based conflict detection and elimination. Eur. J. Oper. Res. 275(2), 737–754 (2019)")); _(iv) cost management:_ diverse consensus models with minimum cost have been already proposed to address this challenge, which is associated to the feedback mechanism of the whole process; _(v) knowledge distribution and information increase:_ this concerns the diverse social relationships that may exist among decision makers as well as the consideration of additional information such as trust and reputation of them.  
最先进的方法试图解决以下主要挑战（Tang和Liao， [2019](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-031-30694-5_23?utm_source=chatgpt.com#ref-CR19 "Tang, M., Liao, H.: From conventional group decision making to large-scale group decision making: what are the challenges and how to meet them in big data era? A state-of-the-art survey. Omega 102141 (2019). https://doi.org/10.1016/j.omega.2019.102141") ）：（ _i）减少决策者维度：_聚类分析是迄今为止使用最广泛的方法，旨在降低复杂性相关问题的成本，以及确定共同的意见模式（例如具有相似意见的集群和代表每个集群的发言人）； _(ii) 决策信息的加权和聚合：_开发一种合理的方法来考虑个体和子群体的不同特征来确定权重非常关键，使得算术平均或加权平均等简单的聚合策略不合适； _（iii）参与者行为的管理：_现有研究往往采用社交网络分析的视角来研究决策者之间达成共识的过程以及相关的冲突检测和消除（Liu _et al._ ， [2019](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-031-30694-5_23?utm_source=chatgpt.com#ref-CR15 "Liu, B.S., Zhou, Q., Ding, R.X., Palomares, I., Herrera, F.: Large-scale group decision making model based on social network analysis: trust relationship-based conflict detection and elimination. Eur. J. Oper. Res. 275(2), 737–754 (2019)") ）； _(iv) 成本管理：_已经提出了多种成本最低的共识模型来应对这一挑战，这与整个流程的反馈机制有关； _(v) 知识传播和信息增加：_这涉及决策者之间可能存在的多样化社会关系以及对决策者的信任和声誉等额外信息的考虑



### .2 Conceptual Architecture  
3.2概念架构

The proposed platform offers a holistic and modular solution that securely hosts and effectively supports large-scale deliberation processes. All the individual modules are designed to be built on top of a cloud service system, configured to be aligned with the needs of all types of stakeholders. This modular approach constitutes the backbone of our solution, which is capable of thoroughly addressing the complexity of deliberative processes, while also enhancing trust, transparency and legitimacy of policy making.  
拟议的平台提供了一个整体和模块化的解决方案，可以安全地托管并有效地支持大规模的审议过程。所有单独的模块都设计为构建在云服务系统之上，并配置为满足所有类型利益相关者的需求。这种模块化方法构成了我们解决方案的支柱，它能够彻底解决审议过程的复杂性，同时还能增强政策制定的信任、透明度和合法性。

Guided by advancements in (Explainable) AI, ML, NLP, Graph Theory and Argumentation, our human-centric approach will produce an efficient and scalable platform that can support deliberation processes of different models and at all levels, from local to global. The proposed technical solution, whose _three-layer architecture_ is illustrated in Fig. [1](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-031-30694-5_23?utm_source=chatgpt.com#Fig1), ensures the seamless integration (at both a conceptual and a technical level) and interoperability of diverse components and services. It enables a _synergy of human and machine reasoning_ towards facilitating and augmenting the participation and deliberation of diverse types of stakeholders in structured discursive interactions. In addition, it exploits _rich semantics at machine level_ to enable the meaningful incorporation and orchestration of interoperable services, aiming to reduce the inherent data-intensiveness of the context under consideration. In particular, the proposed solution seamlessly integrates:  
在（可解释的）人工智能、机器学习、自然语言处理、图论和论证方面的进步的指导下，我们以人为中心的方法将产生一个高效且可扩展的平台，可以支持从本地到全球的各个级别的不同模型的审议过程。所提出的技术解决方案的_三层架构_如图[1](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-031-30694-5_23?utm_source=chatgpt.com#Fig1)所示，确保了不同组件和服务的无缝集成（在概念和技术层面）和互操作性。它实现了_人类和机器推理的协同作用，_以促进和增强不同类型的利益相关者在结构化话语交互中的参与和审议。此外，它_在机器级别利用丰富的语义_来实现可互操作服务的有意义的合并和编排，旨在减少所考虑的上下文的固有数据密集度。特别是，所提出的解决方案无缝集成：
![[Pasted image 20241124215834.png]]

- **_Participation and deliberation support services_** (Fig. [1](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-031-30694-5_23?utm_source=chatgpt.com#Fig1), top layer) that (i) support incremental formalization of argumentative deliberation, i.e., a stepwise and controlled evolution from a mere collection of individual ideas and resources to the production of highly contextualized and interrelated knowledge artifacts; (ii) augment sense-making through advanced visualization and monitoring dashboards that offer an informative and user-friendly overview of a deliberation process in terms of participants’ engagement and contributed knowledge, while also providing insights about the structure, evolution and dynamics of a deliberation process; (iii) provide advanced knowledge exchange and co-creation functionalities by offering a deliberation environment that supports interpretation of diverse knowledge items and their interrelationships; (iv) are geared towards facilitating collective decision making and consensus building through innovative virtual workspaces that enable participants rank alternative solutions; (v) aid policy makers discover and elucidate key points relevant to the deliberation and accordingly compose evidence-informed policies and practices, and (vi) aid citizens and other stakeholders to get explanations and reporting about the inferential process of the underlying AI algorithms and decision making mechanisms, thus promoting trust in the deliberation outputs.  
    **_参与和审议支持服务_**（图[1](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-031-30694-5_23?utm_source=chatgpt.com#Fig1) ，顶层）：(i) 支持论证审议的增量形式化，即从单纯收集个人想法和资源到生产高度情境化和相互关联的知识工件的逐步和受控的演变; (ii) 通过先进的可视化和监控仪表板增强意义构建，这些仪表板在参与者的参与和贡献的知识方面提供了审议过程的信息丰富且用户友好的概述，同时还提供了有关审议的结构、演变和动态的见解过程; (iii) 通过提供支持解释不同知识项目及其相互关系的审议环境，提供先进的知识交流和共同创造功能； (iv) 旨在通过创新的虚拟工作空间促进集体决策和建立共识，使参与者能够对替代解决方案进行排名； (v) 帮助政策制定者发现和阐明与审议相关的关键点，并相应地制定基于证据的政策和实践，以及 (vi) 帮助公民和其他利益相关者获得有关底层人工智能算法和决策的推理过程的解释和报告制定机制，从而促进对审议成果的信任。
    
- **_Knowledge processing services_** (Fig. [1](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-031-30694-5_23?utm_source=chatgpt.com#Fig1), middle layer) that enable a sophisticated analysis on the associated textual content of deliberative processes. Building on prominent AI techniques, this set of services facilitates the comprehension of the structure and meaning of argumentative deliberation by breaking down the input received into a machine-readable format. By understanding a set of linguistic and structural cues, our solution enables a precise interpretation of the corresponding texts and their transformation into actionable, measurable and easily accessible knowledge, thus augmenting the quality of human-computer interaction. Items identified populate and are meaningfully linked with the platform’s knowledge graph to support a sophisticated representation of deliberation entities and their dynamics. This set of services builds on and extends state-of-the-art ML frameworks and neural architectures for NLP to harness the complexity and address the uncertainties stemming from the associated data and knowledge. It includes services that (i) deploy novel argumentation mining mechanisms paying particular attention to argumentation quality; (ii) trigger context-dedicated argumentation aggregation algorithms to serve the clustering of similar deliberation items, as well as the consolidation and homogenization of participants’ input by leveraging prominent text summarisation techniques; (iii) enable opinion mining techniques to identify, extract and process opinions from text by using a lexical approach in combination with prominent ML/NLP techniques, and (iv) handle conflict detection by analyzing the results of argument mining and offering recommendations for conflict resolution.  
    **_知识处理服务_**（图[1](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-031-30694-5_23?utm_source=chatgpt.com#Fig1) ，中间层）能够对审议过程的相关文本内容进行复杂的分析。这套服务建立在著名的人工智能技术的基础上，通过将收到的输入分解为机器可读的格式，有助于理解论证审议的结构和含义。通过理解一组语言和结构线索，我们的解决方案能够精确解释相应的文本，并将其转化为可操作、可测量和易于获取的知识，从而提高人机交互的质量。识别出的项目会填充并与平台的知识图有意义地链接，以支持审议实体及其动态的复杂表示。这套服务构建并扩展了最先进的 ML 框架和 NLP 神经架构，以利用复杂性并解决相关数据和知识带来的不确定性。它包括以下服务：(i) 部署新颖的论证挖掘机制，特别关注论证质量； (ii) 触发上下文专用的论证聚合算法，以服务于相似审议项目的聚类，以及通过利用突出的文本摘要技术来整合和同质化参与者的输入； (iii) 通过使用词汇方法与著名的 ML/NLP 技术相结合，使意见挖掘技术能够识别、提取和处理文本中的意见，以及 (iv) 通过分析论点挖掘的结果并提供冲突解决建议来处理冲突检测。
    
- **_Data management services_** (Fig. [1](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-031-30694-5_23?utm_source=chatgpt.com#Fig1), bottom layer) that enable the purposeful monitoring and collection and efficient pre-processing of tractable information that exists in our solution’s data sources. Transformation of different kinds of textual documents into a canonical form, structuring of these documents from layout information (e.g., detection of comments and supplementary material), data cleansing (e.g., removing noise from inputs, discarding useless parts of the documents), as well as linguistic annotations that facilitate data indexing are some of the functionalities foreseen in this category of services.  
    **_数据管理服务_**（图[1](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-031-30694-5_23?utm_source=chatgpt.com#Fig1) ，底层）可对我们解决方案的数据源中存在的易处理信息进行有目的的监控和收集以及高效的预处理。将不同类型的文本文档转换为规范形式，根据布局信息构建这些文档（例如，检测评论和补充材料），数据清理（例如，消除输入中的噪音，丢弃文档中无用的部分），以及因为促进数据索引的语言注释是此类服务中预见的一些功能。


# Exponential-Family Random Graph Models for Multi-Layer Networks
https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7?utm_source=chatgpt.com
Studying social processes unfolding in networks consisting of a common set of actors incident on multiple types of relationships has long been of interest across the social sciences. Variously called _multivariate_ or _multiplex_, _multi-item_, and _multi-relational_ networks (Fienberg et al. [1980](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR6 "Fienberg, S. E., Meyer, M. M., & Wasserman, S. S. (1980). Analyzing data from multivariate directed graphs: An application to social networks. In V. Barnett (Ed.), Interpreting multivariate data. London: Wiley."); Frank and Shafie [2016](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR8 "Frank, O., & Shafie, T. (2016). Multivariate entropy analysis of network data. Bulletin of Sociological Methodology/Bulletin de Méthodologie Sociologique, 129(1), 45–63. 
https://doi.org/10.1177/0759106315615511
."); Jeub et al. [2017](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR17 "Jeub, L. G. S., Mahoney, M. W., Mucha, P. J., & Porter, M. A. (2017). A local perspective on community structure in multilayer networks. Network Science, 5(2), 144–163. 
https://doi.org/10.1017/nws.2016.22
."); Pattison [1982](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR32 "Pattison, P. E. (1982). The analysis of semigroups of multirelational systems. Journal of Mathematical Psychology, 25(2), 87–118. 
https://doi.org/10.1016/0022-2496(82)90008-6
."); Voros and Snijders [2017](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR43 "Voros, A., & Snijders, T. A. (2017). Cluster analysis of multiplex networks: Defining composite network measures. Social Networks, 49, 93–112. 
https://doi.org/10.1016/j.socnet.2017.01.002
.")), these social structures typically involve connections among actors on more than one type of binary relationship, which are conceptually “stacked” into layers (Magnani and Wasserman [2017](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR30 "Magnani, M., & Wasserman, S. S. (2017). Introduction to the special issue on multilayer networks. Network Science, 5(2), 141–143. 
https://doi.org/10.1017/nws.2017.15
.")). This type of layered network data can be used to address research questions about social structure and processes that may unfold both within and between layers. Multi-layer models would allow one to consider questions such as: what is the likelihood of forming a friendship tie given the presence of a trust tie between two actors? Do friendships tend to form between actors who consider the same people to be trustworthy? Previous network analytic approaches to multi-layer networks include a combination of covariance-based measures (i.e., correlation, singular value decomposition, canonical correlation), descriptive measures (i.e., joint density, multiplexity, edit distance) and model-based inference (i.e., entailment analysis, stochastic block models, network regression and two-layer exponential-family random graph models). These important foundational techniques are limited in that they provide few tools for analyzing cross-layer structural effects that are often of substantive interest to researchers. Moreover, methods that handle association across many network layers jointly while considering structural properties both within and between layers are not currently available. This paper addresses these gaps by building upon the foundations of multi-layer network analysis.  
研究由一组共同的参与者组成的网络中展开的社会过程，这些参与者发生在多种类型的关系上，长期以来一直引起整个社会科学的兴趣。这些社会结构被称为_多元_或多_路_、_多项目_和_多关系_网络（Fienberg et al. [1980](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR6 "Fienberg, S. E., Meyer, M. M., & Wasserman, S. S. (1980). Analyzing data from multivariate directed graphs: An application to social networks. In V. Barnett (Ed.), Interpreting multivariate data. London: Wiley.") ；Frank and Shafie [2016](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR8 "Frank, O., & Shafie, T. (2016). Multivariate entropy analysis of network data. Bulletin of Sociological Methodology/Bulletin de Méthodologie Sociologique, 129(1), 45–63. https://doi.org/10.1177/0759106315615511 .") ；Jeub et al. [2017](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR17 "Jeub, L. G. S., Mahoney, M. W., Mucha, P. J., & Porter, M. A. (2017). A local perspective on community structure in multilayer networks. Network Science, 5(2), 144–163. https://doi.org/10.1017/nws.2016.22 .") ；Pattison [1982](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR32 "Pattison, P. E. (1982). The analysis of semigroups of multirelational systems. Journal of Mathematical Psychology, 25(2), 87–118. https://doi.org/10.1016/0022-2496(82)90008-6 .") ；Voros and Snijders [2017](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR43 "Voros, A., & Snijders, T. A. (2017). Cluster analysis of multiplex networks: Defining composite network measures. Social Networks, 49, 93–112. https://doi.org/10.1016/j.socnet.2017.01.002 .") ），这些社会结构通常涉及参与者之间的联系不止一种类型的二元关系，这些关系在概念上“堆叠”成层（Magnani 和沃瑟曼[2017](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR30 "Magnani, M., & Wasserman, S. S. (2017). Introduction to the special issue on multilayer networks. Network Science, 5(2), 141–143. https://doi.org/10.1017/nws.2017.15 .") ）。这种类型的分层网络数据可用于解决有关可能在层内和层间展开的社会结构和过程的研究问题。多层模型允许人们考虑以下问题：鉴于两个参与者之间存在信任关系，形成友谊关系的可能性有多大？认为同一个人值得信赖的演员之间是否容易形成友谊？先前的多层网络的网络分析方法包括基于协方差的测量（即相关性、奇异值分解、典型相关性）、描述性测量（即联合密度、复用性、编辑距离）和基于模型的推理（即、蕴含分析、随机块模型、网络回归和两层指数族随机图模型）。这些重要的基础技术的局限性在于，它们提供的用于分析跨层结构效应的工具很少，而研究人员通常对这些效应有实质性兴趣。 此外，目前尚不存在在考虑层内和层间结构属性的同时联合处理跨多个网络层的关联的方法。本文通过建立多层网络分析的基础来解决这些差距。

### 1.1 Previous Work on Multi-Layer Exponential-Family Random Graph Models  
1.1多层指数族随机图模型的前期工作

There is a long history of random graph approaches for modeling both local and global structures within observed network systems, the majority of which focus on single binary relations (Erdős and Rényi [1959](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR5 "Erdős, P., & Rényi, A. (1959). On random graphs. Publicationes Mathematicae Debrecen, 6, 290–297."); Fienberg and Wasserman [1981](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR7 "Fienberg, S., & Wasserman, S. S. (1981). Categorical data analysis of single sociometric relations. Sociological Methodology, 12, 156–192. 
https://doi.org/10.2307/270741
."); Frank and Strauss [1986](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR9 "Frank, O., & Strauss, D. (1986). Markov graphs. Journal of the American Statistical Association, 81(395), 832–842. 
https://doi.org/10.1080/01621459.1986.10478342
."); Holland and Leinhardt [1981](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR11 "Holland, P. W., & Leinhardt, S. (1981). An exponential family of probability distributions for directed graphs. Journal of the American Statistical Association, 76(373), 33–50. 
https://doi.org/10.1080/01621459.1981.10477598
."); Wasserman and Pattison [1996](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR47 "Wasserman, S. S., & Pattison, P. E. (1996). Logit models and logistic regressions for social networks: I. An introduction to markov graphs and p*. Psychometrika, 61(3), 401–425. 
https://doi.org/10.1007/BF02294547
.")). However, network processes, particularly when considering relationships that span great lengths of time between actors, often involve multiple relations. To investigate associations among those multiple relations, methods used include relational algebras and block modeling approaches (Barbillon et al. [2017](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR1 "Barbillon, P., Donnet, S., Lazega, E., & Bar-Hen, A. (2017). Stochastic block models for multiplex networks: An application to a multilevel network of researchers. Journal of the Royal Statistical Society: Series A (Statistics in Society), 180(1), 295–314. 
https://doi.org/10.1111/rssa.12193
."); Boorman and White [1976](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR2 "Boorman, S. A., & White, H. C. (1976). Social structure from multiple networks. II. Role structures. American Journal of Sociology, 81(6), 1384–1446. 
https://doi.org/10.1086/226228
."); Pattison [1982](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR32 "Pattison, P. E. (1982). The analysis of semigroups of multirelational systems. Journal of Mathematical Psychology, 25(2), 87–118. 
https://doi.org/10.1016/0022-2496(82)90008-6
."); White and Reitz [1983](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR49 "White, D. R., & Reitz, K. P. (1983). Graph and semigroup homomorphisms on networks of relations.
https://doi.org/10.1016/0378-8733(83)90025-4
."); White et al. [1976](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR50 "White, H. C., Boorman, S. A., & Breiger, R. L. (1976). Social structure from multiple networks. I. Blockmodels of roles and positions. American Journal of Sociology, 81(4), 730–780. 
https://doi.org/10.1086/226141
.")), correlational approaches (Krackardt [1987](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR23 "Krackardt, D. (1987). QAP partialling as a test of spuriousness. Social Networks, 9(2), 171–186. 
https://doi.org/10.1016/0022-2496(82)90008-6
."); Wasserman et al. [1990](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR46 "Wasserman, S. S., Faust, K., & Galaskiewicz, J. (1990). Correspondence and canonical analysis of relational data. Journal of Mathematical Sociology, 15(1), 11–64. 
https://doi.org/10.1080/0022250X.1990.9990060
.")), and comparisons to null distributions, such as multivariate uniform graph distributions (Fienberg and Wasserman [1981](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR7 "Fienberg, S., & Wasserman, S. S. (1981). Categorical data analysis of single sociometric relations. Sociological Methodology, 12, 156–192. 
https://doi.org/10.2307/270741
.")). Extensions have been developed that considered local structural characteristics within a stochastic modeling framework were initiated over 30 years ago where the dyadic independence model was augmented to incorporate multiple relations (Wasserman [1987](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR45 "Wasserman, S. S. (1987). Conformity of two sociometric relations. Psychometrika, 52(1), 3–18. 
https://doi.org/10.1007/BF02293953
.")). The stochastic block models of Nowicki and Snijders ([2001](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR31 "Nowicki, K., & Snijders, T. A. (2001). Estimation and prediction for stochastic blockstructures. Journal of the American Statistical Association, 96(455), 1077–1087. 
https://doi.org/10.1198/016214501753208735
.")) incorporated multi-layered relations. In the 1990s, Wasserman and Pattison ([1996](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR47 "Wasserman, S. S., & Pattison, P. E. (1996). Logit models and logistic regressions for social networks: I. An introduction to markov graphs and p*. Psychometrika, 61(3), 401–425. 
https://doi.org/10.1007/BF02294547
.")) adapted random graph models of Frank and Strauss ([1986](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR9 "Frank, O., & Strauss, D. (1986). Markov graphs. Journal of the American Statistical Association, 81(395), 832–842. 
https://doi.org/10.1080/01621459.1986.10478342
.")) to larger network systems with more complicated dependence structures and made innovations in parameter estimation. With these newly specified p∗ models, or ERGMs, came the potential to move beyond dyadic independence and to hypothesize and fit models with more complex dependence structures. In so doing, the door was opened to consider the potential for such hypothesized dependencies to be characterized by interdependent relations of different types (Koehly and Pattison [2005](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR22 "Koehly, L. M., & Pattison, P. (2005). Random graph models for social networks: Multiple relations or multiple raters. In P. Carrington, J. Scott, & S. Wasserman (Eds.), Models and methods in social network analysis (pp. 162–191). Cambridge: Cambridge University Press. 
https://doi.org/10.1017/CBO9780511811395.009
.")).  
用于对观察到的网络系统中的局部和全局结构进行建模的随机图方法有着悠久的历史，其中大多数集中于单一二元关系（Erdős 和 Rényi [1959](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR5 "Erdős, P., & Rényi, A. (1959). On random graphs. Publicationes Mathematicae Debrecen, 6, 290–297.") ；Fienberg 和 Wasserman [1981](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR7 "Fienberg, S., & Wasserman, S. S. (1981). Categorical data analysis of single sociometric relations. Sociological Methodology, 12, 156–192. https://doi.org/10.2307/270741 .") ；Frank 和 Strauss [1986](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR9 "Frank, O., & Strauss, D. (1986). Markov graphs. Journal of the American Statistical Association, 81(395), 832–842. https://doi.org/10.1080/01621459.1986.10478342 .") ；Holland 和 Leinhardt [1981）](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR11 "Holland, P. W., & Leinhardt, S. (1981). An exponential family of probability distributions for directed graphs. Journal of the American Statistical Association, 76(373), 33–50. https://doi.org/10.1080/01621459.1981.10477598 .")沃瑟曼和帕蒂森[1996](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR47 "Wasserman, S. S., & Pattison, P. E. (1996). Logit models and logistic regressions for social networks: I. An introduction to markov graphs and p*. Psychometrika, 61(3), 401–425. https://doi.org/10.1007/BF02294547 .") ）。然而，网络过程，特别是当考虑参与者之间跨越很长一段时间的关系时，通常涉及多种关系。为了研究这些多重关系之间的关联，所使用的方法包括关系代数和块建模方法（Barbillon et al. [2017](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR1 "Barbillon, P., Donnet, S., Lazega, E., & Bar-Hen, A. (2017). Stochastic block models for multiplex networks: An application to a multilevel network of researchers. Journal of the Royal Statistical Society: Series A (Statistics in Society), 180(1), 295–314. https://doi.org/10.1111/rssa.12193 .") ；Boorman and White [1976](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR2 "Boorman, S. A., & White, H. C. (1976). Social structure from multiple networks. II. Role structures. American Journal of Sociology, 81(6), 1384–1446. https://doi.org/10.1086/226228 .") ；Pattison [1982](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR32 "Pattison, P. E. (1982). The analysis of semigroups of multirelational systems. Journal of Mathematical Psychology, 25(2), 87–118. https://doi.org/10.1016/0022-2496(82)90008-6 .") ；White and Reitz [1983](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR49 "White, D. R., & Reitz, K. P. (1983). Graph and semigroup homomorphisms on networks of relations. https://doi.org/10.1016/0378-8733(83)90025-4 .") ；White et al. [1976](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR50 "White, H. C., Boorman, S. A., & Breiger, R. L. (1976). Social structure from multiple networks. I. Blockmodels of roles and positions. American Journal of Sociology, 81(4), 730–780. https://doi.org/10.1086/226141 .") ）、相关方法（Krackardt [1987](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR23 "Krackardt, D. (1987). QAP partialling as a test of spuriousness. Social Networks, 9(2), 171–186. https://doi.org/10.1016/0022-2496(82)90008-6 .") ； Wasserman 等人[1990](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR46 "Wasserman, S. S., Faust, K., & Galaskiewicz, J. (1990). Correspondence and canonical analysis of relational data. Journal of Mathematical Sociology, 15(1), 11–64. https://doi.org/10.1080/0022250X.1990.9990060 .") ），以及与 null 的比较分布，例如多元均匀图分布（Fienberg 和 Wasserman [1981](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR7 "Fienberg, S., & Wasserman, S. S. (1981). Categorical data analysis of single sociometric relations. Sociological Methodology, 12, 156–192. https://doi.org/10.2307/270741 .") ）。 30 多年前，人们开始对随机建模框架内的局部结构特征进行扩展，其中二元独立模型被增强以纳入多种关系（Wasserman [1987](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR45 "Wasserman, S. S. (1987). Conformity of two sociometric relations. Psychometrika, 52(1), 3–18. https://doi.org/10.1007/BF02293953 .") ）。 Nowicki 和 Snijders ( [2001](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR31 "Nowicki, K., & Snijders, T. A. (2001). Estimation and prediction for stochastic blockstructures. Journal of the American Statistical Association, 96(455), 1077–1087. https://doi.org/10.1198/016214501753208735 .") ) 的随机块模型结合了多层关系。 20世纪90年代，Wasserman和Pattison（ [1996](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR47 "Wasserman, S. S., & Pattison, P. E. (1996). Logit models and logistic regressions for social networks: I. An introduction to markov graphs and p*. Psychometrika, 61(3), 401–425. https://doi.org/10.1007/BF02294547 .") ）将Frank和Strauss（ [1986](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR9 "Frank, O., & Strauss, D. (1986). Markov graphs. Journal of the American Statistical Association, 81(395), 832–842. https://doi.org/10.1080/01621459.1986.10478342 .") ）的随机图模型改编成具有更复杂依赖结构的更大网络系统，并在参数估计方面进行了创新。 有了这些新指定的p∗模型（ERGM），就有可能超越二元独立性，并假设和拟合具有更复杂依赖结构的模型。这样做，为考虑这种假设的依赖关系的可能性打开了大门，这些依赖关系以不同类型的相互依赖关系为特征（Koehly 和 Pattison [2005](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR22 "Koehly, L. M., & Pattison, P. (2005). Random graph models for social networks: Multiple relations or multiple raters. In P. Carrington, J. Scott, & S. Wasserman (Eds.), Models and methods in social network analysis (pp. 162–191). Cambridge: Cambridge University Press. https://doi.org/10.1017/CBO9780511811395.009 .") ）。

In the late 1990s, ERGMs were applied to several multivariate network datasets, most notably resource exchanges among lawyers in Lazega’s classic dataset (Lazega and Pattison [1999](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR28 "Lazega, E., & Pattison, P. E. (1999). Multiplexity, generalized exchange and cooperation in organizations: A case study. Social Networks, 21(1), 67–90. 
https://doi.org/10.1016/S0378-8733(99)00002-7
.")). These models were also redefined to consider temporal networks, with longitudinal measurements on the same relations (Robins and Pattison [2001](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR33 "Robins, G., & Pattison, P. E. (2001). Random graph models for temporal processes in social networks. Journal of Mathematical Sociology, 25, 5–41. 
https://doi.org/10.1080/0022250X.2001.9990243
.")). Lazega and Pattison ([1999](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR28 "Lazega, E., & Pattison, P. E. (1999). Multiplexity, generalized exchange and cooperation in organizations: A case study. Social Networks, 21(1), 67–90. 
https://doi.org/10.1016/S0378-8733(99)00002-7
.")), in particular, proposed an initial taxonomy of possible triad configurations for directed networks. Unfortunately, the type of triad-based specification used has since been found to induce poorly behaved models in a phenomenon that has come to be called _degeneracy_ (Handcock [2003](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR10 "Handcock, M. S. (2003). Assessing degeneracy in statistical models of social networks (Working Paper No. 39). Seattle, WA: Center for Statistics; the Social Sciences, University of Washington. 
http://www.csss.washington.edu/Papers/
."); Schweinberger [2011](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR35 "Schweinberger, M. (2011). Instability, sensitivity, and degeneracy of discrete exponential families. Journal of the American Statistical Association, 106(496), 1361–1370. 
https://doi.org/10.1198/jasa.2011.tm10747
.")). In the paper of Lazega and Pattison ([1999](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR28 "Lazega, E., & Pattison, P. E. (1999). Multiplexity, generalized exchange and cooperation in organizations: A case study. Social Networks, 21(1), 67–90. 
https://doi.org/10.1016/S0378-8733(99)00002-7
.")), it may have been masked by their use of maximum pseudo-likelihood estimation (MPLE) (Strauss and Ikeda [1990](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR42 "Strauss, D., & Ikeda, M. (1990). Pseudolikelihood estimation for social networks. Journal of the American Statistical Association, 85(409), 204–212. 
https://doi.org/10.1080/01621459.1981.10477598
.")) as opposed to the more accurate MCMC-based methods (Hunter and Handcock [2006](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR15 "Hunter, D. R., & Handcock, M. S. (2006). Inference in curved exponential family models for networks. Journal of Computational and Graphical Statistics, 15(3), 565–583. 
https://doi.org/10.1198/106186006X133069
."); Snijders [2002](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR38 "Snijders, T. A. (2002). Markov chain Monte Carlo estimation of exponential random graph models. Journal of Social Structure, 3(2), 1–40.")) that were developed a few years later. (Schweinberger et al. ([2020](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR36 "Schweinberger, M., Krivitsky, P. N., Butts, C. T., & Stewart, J. (2020). Exponential-family models of random graphs: Inference in finite-, super-, and infinite population scenarios. Statistical Science, To appear. 
arXiv: 1707.04800")) provide a more detailed historical account.) A more recent chapter by Wang ([2012](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR44 "Wang, P. (2012). Exponential random graph model extensions: Models for multiple networks and bipartite networks. In D. Lusher, J. Koskinen, & G. Robins (Eds.), Exponential random graph models for social networks: Theory, methods, and applications (pp. 115–129). Cambridge: Cambridge University Press. 
https://doi.org/10.1017/CBO9780511894701.012
.")) described a number of specifications for two-layer networks, reviewing the models introduced by Lazega and Pattison ([1999](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR28 "Lazega, E., & Pattison, P. E. (1999). Multiplexity, generalized exchange and cooperation in organizations: A case study. Social Networks, 21(1), 67–90. 
https://doi.org/10.1016/S0378-8733(99)00002-7
.")) and introducing two-layer extensions of the nondegenerate specifications of (Snijders et al. [2006](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR40 "Snijders, T. A., Pattison, P. E., Robins, G. L., & Handcock, M. S. (2006). New specifications for exponential random graph models. Sociological Methodology, 36(1), 99–153. 
https://doi.org/10.1111/j.1467-9531.2006.00176.x
.")), implemented in the XPNet software.  
在 20 世纪 90 年代末，ERGM 被应用于多个多元网络数据集，最引人注目的是 Lazega 经典数据集中律师之间的资源交换（Lazega 和 Pattison [1999](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR28 "Lazega, E., & Pattison, P. E. (1999). Multiplexity, generalized exchange and cooperation in organizations: A case study. Social Networks, 21(1), 67–90. https://doi.org/10.1016/S0378-8733(99)00002-7 .") ）。这些模型也被重新定义以考虑时间网络，并对相同关系进行纵向测量（Robins 和 Pattison [2001](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR33 "Robins, G., & Pattison, P. E. (2001). Random graph models for temporal processes in social networks. Journal of Mathematical Sociology, 25, 5–41. https://doi.org/10.1080/0022250X.2001.9990243 .") ）。 Lazega 和 Pattison ( [1999](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR28 "Lazega, E., & Pattison, P. E. (1999). Multiplexity, generalized exchange and cooperation in organizations: A case study. Social Networks, 21(1), 67–90. https://doi.org/10.1016/S0378-8733(99)00002-7 .") ) 特别提出了有向网络可能的三元组配置的初始分类法。不幸的是，后来发现所使用的基于三元组的规范类型会导致模型表现不佳，这种现象被称为_简并性_（Handcock [2003](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR10 "Handcock, M. S. (2003). Assessing degeneracy in statistical models of social networks (Working Paper No. 39). Seattle, WA: Center for Statistics; the Social Sciences, University of Washington. http://www.csss.washington.edu/Papers/ .") ；Schweinberger [2011](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR35 "Schweinberger, M. (2011). Instability, sensitivity, and degeneracy of discrete exponential families. Journal of the American Statistical Association, 106(496), 1361–1370. https://doi.org/10.1198/jasa.2011.tm10747 .") ）。在 Lazega 和 Pattison（ [1999](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR28 "Lazega, E., & Pattison, P. E. (1999). Multiplexity, generalized exchange and cooperation in organizations: A case study. Social Networks, 21(1), 67–90. https://doi.org/10.1016/S0378-8733(99)00002-7 .") ）的论文中，它可能被他们使用最大伪似然估计（MPLE）（Strauss 和 Ikeda [1990](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR42 "Strauss, D., & Ikeda, M. (1990). Pseudolikelihood estimation for social networks. Journal of the American Statistical Association, 85(409), 204–212. https://doi.org/10.1080/01621459.1981.10477598 .") ）所掩盖，而不是更准确的基于 MCMC 的方法（Hunter 和 Handcock [2006](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR15 "Hunter, D. R., & Handcock, M. S. (2006). Inference in curved exponential family models for networks. Journal of Computational and Graphical Statistics, 15(3), 565–583. https://doi.org/10.1198/106186006X133069 .") ； Snijders [2002](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR38 "Snijders, T. A. (2002). Markov chain Monte Carlo estimation of exponential random graph models. Journal of Social Structure, 3(2), 1–40.") ）是几年后开发的。 （Schweinberger 等人（ [2020](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR36 "Schweinberger, M., Krivitsky, P. N., Butts, C. T., & Stewart, J. (2020). Exponential-family models of random graphs: Inference in finite-, super-, and infinite population scenarios. Statistical Science, To appear. arXiv: 1707.04800") ）提供了更详细的历史记录。）Wang（ [2012](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR44 "Wang, P. (2012). Exponential random graph model extensions: Models for multiple networks and bipartite networks. In D. Lusher, J. Koskinen, & G. Robins (Eds.), Exponential random graph models for social networks: Theory, methods, and applications (pp. 115–129). Cambridge: Cambridge University Press. https://doi.org/10.1017/CBO9780511894701.012 .") ）最近的一章描述了两层网络的许多规范，回顾了 Lazega 和 Pattison（ [1999](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR28 "Lazega, E., & Pattison, P. E. (1999). Multiplexity, generalized exchange and cooperation in organizations: A case study. Social Networks, 21(1), 67–90. https://doi.org/10.1016/S0378-8733(99)00002-7 .") ）引入的模型，并介绍了两种(Snijders et al. [2006](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR40 "Snijders, T. A., Pattison, P. E., Robins, G. L., & Handcock, M. S. (2006). New specifications for exponential random graph models. Sociological Methodology, 36(1), 99–153. https://doi.org/10.1111/j.1467-9531.2006.00176.x .") ) 的非简并规范的层扩展，在XPNet软件中实现。

Ultimately, applications that consider multi-layer networks are still limited, due, largely, to the increased complexity of and inability to fit such multi-layer models with more than a few relations of interest. Given the complex social worlds within which we live and the importance of interpersonal mechanisms on health, well-being, and mortality (Holt-Lunstad et al. [2010](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR12 "Holt-Lunstad, J., Smith, T., & Layton, J. (2010). Social relationships and mortality risk: A meta-analytic review. PLoS Medicine, 7(7), e1000316. 
https://doi.org/10.1371/journal.pmed.1000316
.")), development of models to understand how varying types of social ties are structured has important implications. As such, there has been significant effort within the community toward identifying methodological approaches to characterize these complex social systems. Moreover, one of the advantages of estimating joint models with many layers—rather than simply fitting separate ERGMs for each layer—is that within-model contrasts between differences in social processes at play in the separate layers can be evaluated.  
最终，考虑多层网络的应用程序仍然受到限制，这在很大程度上是由于复杂性的增加以及无法将此类多层模型与多个感兴趣的关系相匹配。鉴于我们生活的复杂社会世界以及人际机制对健康、福祉和死亡率的重要性（Holt-Lunstad 等， [2010](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR12 "Holt-Lunstad, J., Smith, T., & Layton, J. (2010). Social relationships and mortality risk: A meta-analytic review. PLoS Medicine, 7(7), e1000316. https://doi.org/10.1371/journal.pmed.1000316 .") ），开发模型来理解不同类型的社会关系如何构建具有重要意义。因此，社区内部做出了巨大的努力来确定表征这些复杂社会系统的方法论。此外，估计多层联合模型（而不是简单地为每一层拟合单独的 ERGM）的优点之一是，可以评估不同层中发挥作用的社会过程差异之间的模型内对比。

These methodological advances bring with them some challenges to implementation. First, as discussed by Voros and Snijders ([2017](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR43 "Voros, A., & Snijders, T. A. (2017). Cluster analysis of multiplex networks: Defining composite network measures. Social Networks, 49, 93–112. 
https://doi.org/10.1016/j.socnet.2017.01.002
.")), the number of structural parameters that can characterize a structural model increases exponentially as the number of layers defining the system increases. As such, there is a plethora of interpersonal mechanisms that may explain potential cross-layer dependencies requiring model specification to be hypothesis driven and grounded in theory. Second, logistical and computational aspects related to model specification and estimation become more complicated in multi-layer contexts, particularly when one is aiming to move beyond correlation between layers. There has been success in implementing such models with just a few relational layers, including among one-mode multi-layer networks and between two-mode and one-mode networks (Huitsing et al. [2012](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR13 "Huitsing, G., Van Duijn, M. A., Snijders, T. A., Wang, P., Sainio, M., Salmivalli, C., et al. (2012). Univariate and multivariate models of positive and negative networks: Liking, disliking, and bully-victim relationships. Social Networks, 34(4), 645–657. 
https://doi.org/10.1016/j.socnet.2012.08.001
."); Snijders et al. [2013](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR39 "Snijders, T. A., Lomi, A., & Torló, V. J. (2013). A model for the multiplex dynamics of two-mode and one-mode networks, with an application to employment preference, friendship, and advice. Social Networks, 35(2), 265–276. 
https://doi.org/10.1016/j.socnet.2012.05.005
."); Wang [2012](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR44 "Wang, P. (2012). Exponential random graph model extensions: Models for multiple networks and bipartite networks. In D. Lusher, J. Koskinen, & G. Robins (Eds.), Exponential random graph models for social networks: Theory, methods, and applications (pp. 115–129). Cambridge: Cambridge University Press. 
https://doi.org/10.1017/CBO9780511894701.012
.")). But, extensions moving beyond just a few layers are scarce and most of those extensions are limited in their ability to map to hypothesized structural characteristics that might be threaded across layers. For example, Frank and Shafie ([2016](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR8 "Frank, O., & Shafie, T. (2016). Multivariate entropy analysis of network data. Bulletin of Sociological Methodology/Bulletin de Méthodologie Sociologique, 129(1), 45–63. 
https://doi.org/10.1177/0759106315615511
.")) and Shafie ([2015](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR37 "Shafie, T. (2015). A multigraph approach to social network analysis. Journal of Social Structure, 16(1), 1–21.")) consider the use of entropy to identify interdependencies among a set of network variables derived from multigraphs. Salter-Townshend and McCormick [2017](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR34 "Salter-Townshend, M., & McCormick, T. H. (2017). Latent space models for multiview network data. Annals of Applied Statistics, 11(3), 1217–1244. 
https://doi.org/10.1016/j.socnet.2017.01.002
.") propose latent space analysis as a way to understand dependencies across layers conditional on within layer structure. Others have used data reduction approaches, such as cluster analysis, to reduce the dimensionality of layers and, thus, simplify the multigraph problem (Voros and Snijders [2017](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR43 "Voros, A., & Snijders, T. A. (2017). Cluster analysis of multiplex networks: Defining composite network measures. Social Networks, 49, 93–112. 
https://doi.org/10.1016/j.socnet.2017.01.002
.")). And, De Domenico et al. ([2013](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR4 "De Domenico, M., Solè-Ribalta, A., Cozzo, E., Kivelà, M., Moreno, Y., Porter, M. A., et al. (2013). Mathematical formulation of multilayer networks. Physical Review X, 3(4), 041022. 
https://doi.org/10.1103/PhysRevX.3.041022
.")) demonstrate the use of tensor algebra for investigating structural aspects of multi-layer networks that can account for both multiplex relations and temporal dynamics.  
这些方法上的进步给实施带来了一些挑战。首先，正如 Voros 和 Snijders ( [2017](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR43 "Voros, A., & Snijders, T. A. (2017). Cluster analysis of multiplex networks: Defining composite network measures. Social Networks, 49, 93–112. https://doi.org/10.1016/j.socnet.2017.01.002 .") ) 所讨论的，随着定义系统的层数的增加，可以表征结构模型的结构参数的数量呈指数增加。因此，有大量的人际机制可以解释潜在的跨层依赖性，要求模型规范是假设驱动的并以理论为基础。其次，与模型规范和估计相关的逻辑和计算方面在多层上下文中变得更加复杂，特别是当人们的目标是超越层之间的相关性时。仅用几个关系层就可以成功实现此类模型，包括单模多层网络之间以及双模和单模网络之间（Huitsing et al. [2012](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR13 "Huitsing, G., Van Duijn, M. A., Snijders, T. A., Wang, P., Sainio, M., Salmivalli, C., et al. (2012). Univariate and multivariate models of positive and negative networks: Liking, disliking, and bully-victim relationships. Social Networks, 34(4), 645–657. https://doi.org/10.1016/j.socnet.2012.08.001 .") ；Snijders et al. [2013](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR39 "Snijders, T. A., Lomi, A., & Torló, V. J. (2013). A model for the multiplex dynamics of two-mode and one-mode networks, with an application to employment preference, friendship, and advice. Social Networks, 35(2), 265–276. https://doi.org/10.1016/j.socnet.2012.05.005 .") ；Wang [2012](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR44 "Wang, P. (2012). Exponential random graph model extensions: Models for multiple networks and bipartite networks. In D. Lusher, J. Koskinen, & G. Robins (Eds.), Exponential random graph models for social networks: Theory, methods, and applications (pp. 115–129). Cambridge: Cambridge University Press. https://doi.org/10.1017/CBO9780511894701.012 .") ） 。但是，超出几层的扩展很少，并且大多数扩展在映射到可能跨层线程的假设结构特征的能力方面受到限制。例如，Frank 和 Shafie ( [2016](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR8 "Frank, O., & Shafie, T. (2016). Multivariate entropy analysis of network data. Bulletin of Sociological Methodology/Bulletin de Méthodologie Sociologique, 129(1), 45–63. https://doi.org/10.1177/0759106315615511 .") ) 以及 Shafie ( [2015](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR37 "Shafie, T. (2015). A multigraph approach to social network analysis. Journal of Social Structure, 16(1), 1–21.") ) 考虑使用熵来识别从多重图导出的一组网络变量之间的相互依赖性。 Salter-Townshend 和 McCormick [2017](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR34 "Salter-Townshend, M., & McCormick, T. H. (2017). Latent space models for multiview network data. Annals of Applied Statistics, 11(3), 1217–1244. https://doi.org/10.1016/j.socnet.2017.01.002 .")提出潜在空间分析作为理解层间结构内条件的跨层依赖关系的一种方法。其他人使用数据缩减方法（例如聚类分析）来减少层的维数，从而简化多图问题（Voros 和 Snijders [2017](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR43 "Voros, A., & Snijders, T. A. (2017). Cluster analysis of multiplex networks: Defining composite network measures. Social Networks, 49, 93–112. https://doi.org/10.1016/j.socnet.2017.01.002 .") ）。并且，德多梅尼科等人。 ( [2013](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR4 "De Domenico, M., Solè-Ribalta, A., Cozzo, E., Kivelà, M., Moreno, Y., Porter, M. A., et al. (2013). Mathematical formulation of multilayer networks. Physical Review X, 3(4), 041022. https://doi.org/10.1103/PhysRevX.3.041022 .") ) 演示了使用张量代数来研究多层网络的结构方面，可以解释多重关系和时间动态。

These developments notwithstanding, there exists a considerable gap in the theory and estimation of ERGMs for multi-layer networks. In what follows, our contribution builds upon this history from within the ERGM framework. We begin with some notation for multi-layer networks.  
尽管取得了这些进展，多层网络 ERGM 的理论和估计仍存在相当大的差距。接下来，我们的贡献将建立在 ERGM 框架内的这段历史之上。我们从多层网络的一些符号开始。![[截圖 2024-11-24 下午10.09.56.png]]
![[截圖 2024-11-24 下午10.10.16.png]]
## 6 Conclusion  
6结论

This paper introduces new approaches for the analysis of multi-layer networks using ERGMs. Previous work focused largely on modeling just a few layers of multi-relational networks; our contribution applies to an arbitrary number of layers. A new approach for modeling marginal dependence between a set of correlated Bernoulli variables using the Conway–Maxwell–Binomial (CMB) distribution was adapted to the case of ERGMs for multi-layer networks. Additionally, both a _layer logic_ and novel ERGM terms (including nondegenerate shared partners and degree distributions, as well as two-star and two-path terms for multi-layer applications) were introduced, facilitating modeling conditional dependence across—or between—layers. Two empirical examples that consisted of networks with eight and three layers were presented to highlight different aspects of our advances. With these examples, the paper also demonstrated how fitting joint ERGMs to multiple layers—logical or observed—facilitates the use of within-model contrasts to test for differences in the magnitude of coefficients modeling the same social processes across layers.  
本文介绍了使用 ERGM 分析多层网络的新方法。以前的工作主要集中于对多关系网络的几层进行建模；我们的贡献适用于任意数量的层。使用康威-麦克斯韦-二项式 (CMB) 分布对一组相关伯努利变量之间的边际依赖性进行建模的新方法适用于多层网络 ERGM 的情况。此外，还引入了_层逻辑_和新颖的 ERGM 术语（包括非简并共享伙伴和度分布，以及多层应用程序的两星和双路径术语），有助于对层间或层间的条件依赖性进行建模。提出了两个由八层和三层网络组成的实证示例，以强调我们进展的不同方面。通过这些示例，本文还演示了如何将联合 ERGM 拟合到多个层（逻辑层或观察层）如何促进使用模型内对比来测试跨层建模相同社会过程的系数大小的差异。

The results of our empirical example using the Knecht classroom data in Sect. [5.2.2](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#Sec18) demonstrated that there exists a trade-off between using two-layer logical _intersection_ layer specifications (which model well bivariate correlations with a greater number of parameters) and using the CMB specifications (which are better at modeling underlying dependence structure across many layers with fewer parameters). We also demonstrated that our approach can be useful in revealing new features of social structure and process vis-à-vis cross-layer ERGM effects. Specifically, using the Lazega lawyers data in Sect. [5.3.2](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#Sec21), we showed that triadic processes involving two-paths that cross two different layers in each segment may be important for suppressing ties in a third layer, controlling for other within- and cross-layer effects.  
我们使用《Sect.》中的 Knecht 课堂数据进行实证示例的结果。 [5.2.2](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#Sec18)证明，使用两层逻辑_交叉_层规范（可以很好地模拟具有更多参数的二元相关性）和使用 CMB 规范（可以更好地建模跨多个层的底层依赖结构）之间存在权衡参数较少）。我们还证明，我们的方法有助于揭示社会结构和过程相对于跨层 ERGM 效应的新特征。具体来说，使用《Sect.》中的 Lazega 律师数据。 [5.3.2](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#Sec21) ，我们表明，涉及每个段中跨越两个不同层的两条路径的三元过程对于抑制第三层中的联系、控制其他层内和跨层效应可能很重要。

It is important to note that, as presented, these multi-layer ERGMs are best suited for theoretically informed, hypothesis-driven analyses. The number of structural features that can be constructed from the layer logic and through the CMB increases exponentially with the number of layers comprising the network system. Thus, it is important for users of multi-layer ERGMs to be thoughtful about model specification, such that conceptually appropriate and hypothesized structural characteristics define the estimated models. For example, in some scenarios the CMB may represent a theoretically important structural feature of the multi-layer system. These might include the case when multiple raters are informing on a single relation (Koehly and Pattison [2005](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR22 "Koehly, L. M., & Pattison, P. (2005). Random graph models for social networks: Multiple relations or multiple raters. In P. Carrington, J. Scott, & S. Wasserman (Eds.), Models and methods in social network analysis (pp. 162–191). Cambridge: Cambridge University Press. 
https://doi.org/10.1017/CBO9780511811395.009
."); Krackhardt [1987](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR24 "Krackhardt, D. (1987). Cognitive social structures. Social Networks, 9(2), 109–134.")) or multi-item construct networks (Koehly and Marcum [2016](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR21 "Koehly, L. M., & Marcum, C. S. (2016). Multi-relational measurement for latent construct networks. Psychological Methods, 21(4), 1–35. 
https://doi.org/10.1037/met0000110
.")). However, in other scenarios, the layers may be distinct, with totally different meanings (e.g., positive and negative ties); in these scenarios, the CMB may not be meaningful, requiring the use of the layer logic to characterize hypothesized associations across layers.  
值得注意的是，正如所介绍的，这些多层 ERGM 最适合理论上知情、假设驱动的分析。可以从层逻辑并通过 CMB 构建的结构特征的数量随着构成网络系统的层数呈指数增长。因此，多层 ERGM 的用户必须考虑模型规范，以便概念上适当的假设结构特征定义估计模型。例如，在某些场景中，CMB可能代表多层系统理论上重要的结构特征。这些可能包括多个评估者就单一关系提供信息的情况（Koehly 和 Pattison [2005](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR22 "Koehly, L. M., & Pattison, P. (2005). Random graph models for social networks: Multiple relations or multiple raters. In P. Carrington, J. Scott, & S. Wasserman (Eds.), Models and methods in social network analysis (pp. 162–191). Cambridge: Cambridge University Press. https://doi.org/10.1017/CBO9780511811395.009 .") ；Krackhardt [1987](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR24 "Krackhardt, D. (1987). Cognitive social structures. Social Networks, 9(2), 109–134.") ）或多项目构建网络（Koehly 和 Marcum [2016](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR21 "Koehly, L. M., & Marcum, C. S. (2016). Multi-relational measurement for latent construct networks. Psychological Methods, 21(4), 1–35. https://doi.org/10.1037/met0000110 .") ）。然而，在其他情况下，这些层可能是不同的，具有完全不同的含义（例如，积极和消极的联系）；在这些场景中，CMB 可能没有意义，需要使用层逻辑来表征跨层的假设关联。

More generally, while CMB effects behave well in our analyses, more study—both theoretical and simulation—is needed. For example, in Knecht Model 4, the prosocial CMB coefficient is significantly smaller than its antisocial counterpart (δ^=−0.60,p=0.005), but does that mean that there is greater positive association among the antisocial layers? In particular, the number of layers differs between the prosocial and antisocial sets, which may mean that they cannot be compared on an interval scale. And, as we note in Sect. [2](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#Sec6), the effects of heterogeneous layer densities on the CMB statistic require further study as well.  
更一般地说，虽然 CMB 效应在我们的分析中表现良好，但仍需要更多的研究（理论和模拟）。例如，在 Knecht 模型 4 中，亲社会 CMB 系数明显小于其反社会对应系数（ δ^=−0.60,p=0.005 ），但这是否意味着反社会层之间存在更大的正关联？特别是，亲社会集和反社会集之间的层数不同，这可能意味着它们无法在区间尺度上进行比较。而且，正如我们在《教派》中所指出的那样。[如图2](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#Sec6)所示，异质层密度对CMB统计量的影响也需要进一步研究。

Innovations in multi-layer ERGMs that we have introduced here make a clear contribution to advance the field of statistical social network analysis. However, we would be remiss to not mention several limitations and opportunities for future work. First, while in principle our approach is appropriate for an arbitrary number of layers from a theoretical perspective, there are computational and practical limitations that may make estimation infeasible for very complex models with a large number of layers. The burden is on the researcher to ensure that their multi-layer model makes sense for the social processes and structures investigated by the research question at hand. Second, while we address how to apply the principle of marginality to cross-layer triadic effects, realizing carefully written models to that end remains a challenge in maximum likelihood estimation. In part, this is because two-path and two-star effects, on which many triadic closure processes are conditioned, often lead to ERGM degeneracy in general—cross-layer specifications of such terms are apparently not spared from this result based on our supplemental analysis. An alternative to specifying such ideal models is to evaluate how well one’s candidate model replicates features from omitted terms.  
我们在这里介绍的多层 ERGM 的创新为统计社交网络分析领域的发展做出了明显的贡献。然而，如果我们不提及未来工作的一些限制和机会，那就太失职了。首先，虽然从理论上讲，我们的方法原则上适用于任意数量的层，但存在计算和实际限制，可能使得对于具有大量层的非常复杂的模型进行估计不可行。研究人员有责任确保他们的多层模型对于当前研究问题所调查的社会过程和结构有意义。其次，虽然我们解决了如何将边际性原则应用于跨层三元效应，但为此目的实现精心编写的模型仍然是最大似然估计的挑战。在某种程度上，这是因为双路径和双星效应（许多三元闭合过程都以双路径和双星效应为条件）通常会导致 ERGM 简并——根据我们的补充，此类术语的跨层规范显然也无法幸免于这一结果。分析。指定此类理想模型的另一种方法是评估候选模型复制省略项的特征的效果。

For example, in our cross-layer triadic closure model using the Lazega data, we simulated cross-layer two-paths from fitted models and compared the resulting distribution to corresponding two-path values of the observed network. This procedure helps to diagnose how well a higher-order cross-layer triadic term in a model recovers its lower order constituent two-path/two-star terms under simulation. Improvements in estimation for such degeneracy-inducing terms are needed for ERGMs in general and specifically for multi-layer ERGMs where the nascence of these models may inspire new innovations. Second, we have limited our treatment of this family of models to the cross-sectional multi-layer case where we have discussed each layer as representing different social relations. As both Koehly and Pattison ([2005](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR22 "Koehly, L. M., & Pattison, P. (2005). Random graph models for social networks: Multiple relations or multiple raters. In P. Carrington, J. Scott, & S. Wasserman (Eds.), Models and methods in social network analysis (pp. 162–191). Cambridge: Cambridge University Press. 
https://doi.org/10.1017/CBO9780511811395.009
.")) and Snijders et al. ([2013](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR39 "Snijders, T. A., Lomi, A., & Torló, V. J. (2013). A model for the multiplex dynamics of two-mode and one-mode networks, with an application to employment preference, friendship, and advice. Social Networks, 35(2), 265–276. 
https://doi.org/10.1016/j.socnet.2012.05.005
.")) point out, however—by adopting strong theoretical and measurement approaches—the multi-layer ERGM methods can be adapted to multiple rater, or multiple time, assessments of a single relation. Finally, the models we choose to estimate and feature in this paper for our empirical examples may not be ideal from a social theoretic perspective and may suffer from omitted variable biases. Rather than strive for such theoretical niceties, we choose to use the empirical examples to highlight novel features for estimating multi-layer ERGMs that we have introduced here—we at least believe the models to be sensible, if not ideal. We leave ample room for new research questions to be explored using multi-layer ERGMs on these publicly available datasets. Thus, our contributions toward the development of ERGMs for multi-layer networks augment the toolkit from which network scientists may draw in their own research.  
例如，在使用 Lazega 数据的跨层三元闭包模型中，我们根据拟合模型模拟跨层双路径，并将所得分布与观察到的网络的相应双路径值进行比较。此过程有助于诊断模型中的高阶跨层三项项在模拟下恢复其低阶组成双路径/双星项的效果如何。一般来说，ERGM 需要改进对此类简并诱导项的估计，特别是多层 ERGM，这些模型的诞生可能会激发新的创新。其次，我们对这一系列模型的处理仅限于横截面多层案例，其中我们讨论了代表不同社会关系的每一层。正如 Koehly 和 Pattison ( [2005](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR22 "Koehly, L. M., & Pattison, P. (2005). Random graph models for social networks: Multiple relations or multiple raters. In P. Carrington, J. Scott, & S. Wasserman (Eds.), Models and methods in social network analysis (pp. 162–191). Cambridge: Cambridge University Press. https://doi.org/10.1017/CBO9780511811395.009 .") ) 以及 Snijders 等人一样。然而，（ [2013](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s11336-020-09720-7#ref-CR39 "Snijders, T. A., Lomi, A., & Torló, V. J. (2013). A model for the multiplex dynamics of two-mode and one-mode networks, with an application to employment preference, friendship, and advice. Social Networks, 35(2), 265–276. https://doi.org/10.1016/j.socnet.2012.05.005 .") ）指出，通过采用强大的理论和测量方法，多层 ERGM 方法可以适应单个关系的多个评估者或多次评估。最后，我们选择在本文中针对经验示例进行估计和描述的模型从社会理论的角度来看可能并不理想，并且可能会受到遗漏变量偏差的影响。我们没有努力追求这种理论上的精确性，而是选择使用经验示例来突出我们在此介绍的用于估计多层 ERGM 的新特征——我们至少相信这些模型是合理的，即使不是理想的。我们为在这些公开数据集上使用多层 ERGM 来探索新的研究问题留出了充足的空间。因此，我们对多层网络 ERGM 开发的贡献增强了网络科学家可以在自己的研究中借鉴的工具包

# ==Graph Machine Learning in the Era of Large Language Models (LLMs)   大型语言模型（ LLMs ）时代的图机器学习
https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2
![[Pasted image 20241124221313.png]]![[Pasted image 20241124221327.png]]
### 2.1Graph Machine Learning  
2.1图机器学习

As one of the most active fields in artificial intelligence, graph learning has attracted considerable attention to its capability to model complex relationships and structures in data represented as graphs [[44](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib44)]. Nowadays, it has been widely adopted in various applications, including social network analysis [[45](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib45)], protein detection [[46](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib46)], recommender systems [[47](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib47), [48](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib48)], etc.  
作为人工智能最活跃的领域之一，图学习因其对以图表示的数据中的复杂关系和结构进行建模的能力而引起了广泛关注[ [44](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib44) ] 。如今，它已广泛应用于各种应用中，包括社交网络分析[ [45](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib45) ] 、蛋白质检测[ [46](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib46) ] 、推荐系统[[47、48](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib48) []](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib47)等。

The initial phases of graph learning typically use Random Walks, which is a foundational method for exploring graph structures. This technique involves a stochastic process of moving from one node to another within a graph, which is instrumental in understanding node connectivity and influence within networks. Building upon Random Walks, Graph Embedding methods aim to represent nodes (or edges) as low-dimensional vectors while preserving graph topology and node relationships. Representative methods such as LINE [[49](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib49)], DeepWalk [[50](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib50)], and Node2Vec [[51](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib51)] leverage Random Walks to learn node representations, capturing local structures and community information effectively.  
图学习的初始阶段通常使用随机游走，这是探索图结构的基本方法。这项技术涉及在图中从一个节点移动到另一个节点的随机过程，这有助于理解网络中的节点连接性和影响力。基于随机游走的图嵌入方法旨在将节点（或边）表示为低维向量，同时保留图拓扑和节点关系。 LINE [ [49](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib49) ] 、DeepWalk [ [50](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib50) ]和 Node2Vec [ [51](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib51) ]等代表性方法利用随机游走来学习节点表示，有效捕获局部结构和社区信息。

Due to the exceptional representation learning and modeling capabilities, GNNs bolstered by deep learning have brought significant advances in graph learning. For example, GCNs [[52](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib52)] introduce convolutional operations to graph data, enabling effective aggregation of neighborhood information for each node, thus enhancing node representation learning. GraphSAGE [[53](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib53)] learns a function to aggregate information from a node’s local neighborhood in an inductive setting, allowing efficient embedding generation for unseen nodes. GAT [[54](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib54)] further advances GNNs by integrating attention mechanisms, assigning varying weights to nodes in a neighborhood, thereby sharpening the model’s ability to focus on significant nodes. Inspired by the success of transformers [[55](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib55)] in NLP and CV, several studies [[56](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib56), [57](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib57), [58](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib58), [59](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib59), [60](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib60)] adopt self-attention mechanisms to graph data, providing a more global perspective of graph structures and interactions. Recent works [[61](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib61), [62](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib62), [63](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib63), [64](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib64), [65](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib65)] further leverage transformer architectures to enhance graph data modeling. For example, GraphFormer [[61](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib61)] integrates GNN within each layer in the transformer, enabling simultaneous consideration of textual and graph information.  
由于卓越的表示学习和建模能力，深度学习支持的 GNN 为图学习带来了重大进展。例如，GCN [ [52](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib52) ]将卷积运算引入图数据，能够有效聚合每个节点的邻域信息，从而增强节点表示学习。 GraphSAGE [ [53](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib53) ]学习一种在归纳设置中聚合来自节点本地邻域的信息的函数，从而允许对未见过的节点进行高效的嵌入生成。 GAT [ [54](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib54) ]通过集成注意力机制，为邻域中的节点分配不同的权重，从而增强模型关注重要节点的能力，进一步推进了 GNN。受到 NLP 和 CV 中 Transformer [ [55](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib55) ]成功的启发，多项研究[ [56](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib56) , [57](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib57) , [58](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib58) , [59](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib59) , [60](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib60) ]采用自注意力机制来处理图形数据，提供了图形结构和交互的更全局的视角。最近的工作[[](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib65) [61、62、63、64、65](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib64) []](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib61)[进一步](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib62)[利用](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib63)变压器架构来增强图数据建模。例如，GraphFormer [ [61](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib61) ]在转换器的每一层中集成了 GNN，从而能够同时考虑文本和图形信息。

The advancements in LLMs have given rise to graph learning. Recent works [[22](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib22), [66](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib66), [27](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib27), [21](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib21), [67](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib67)] apply techniques from these advanced language models like LLaMA [[24](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib24)] or ChatGPT to graph data, resulting in models capable of understanding and handling graph structures in a manner similar to natural language processing. A typical approach, GraphGPT [[23](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib23)], tokenizes graph data for insertion into LLMs (i.e. Vicuna [[68](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib68)] and LLaMA [[24](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib24)]) thus providing a powerful generalization capability. GLEM [[69](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib69)] further integrates the graph models and LLMs, specifically DeBERTa [[70](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib70)], within a variational Expectation-Maximization (EM) framework. It alternates between updating LLM and GNN in the E-step and M-step, thereby scaling efficiently and improving effectiveness in downstream tasks.  
LLMs的进步催生了图学习。最近[的](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib67)[工作](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib22)[[](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib66) [22,66,27,21,67](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib21) []](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib27)将LLaMA [ [24](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib24) ]或ChatGPT等高级语言模型的技术应用于图数据，从而产生能够以类似于自然语言处理的方式理解和处理图结构的模型。一种典型的方法，GraphGPT [ [23](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib23) ] ，将图数据标记化以插入到LLMs （即 Vicuna [ [68](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib68) ]和 LLaMA [ [24](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib24) ] ）中，从而提供强大的泛化能力。 GLEM [ [69](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib69) ]在变分期望最大化 (EM) 框架内进一步集成了图模型和LLMs ，特别是 DeBERTa [ [70](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib70) ] 。它在 E 步和 M 步中交替更新LLM和 GNN，从而有效扩展并提高下游任务的有效性。

### 2.2Foundation Models (FMs)  
2.2基础模型（FM）

Foundation Models (FMs) represent a significant breakthrough in the field of artificial intelligence, characterized by their ability to be extensively pre-trained on large-scale datasets and adapted to a variety of downstream tasks. These models are distinguished by their extensive pre-training on large-scale datasets and their adaptability to a wide range of downstream tasks. It is worth noting that FMs are not limited to a single field and can be found in natural language [[14](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib14), [15](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib15)], vision [[71](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib71), [72](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib72)], and graph domains [[43](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib43), [19](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib19)], serving as a promising research direction.  
基础模型（FM）代表了人工智能领域的重大突破，其特点是能够在大规模数据集上进行广泛的预训练并适应各种下游任务。这些模型的特点是对大规模数据集进行了广泛的预训练以及对各种下游任务的适应性。值得注意的是，FM并不局限于单一领域，可以在自然语言[ [14,15](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib14) []](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib15) 、视觉[[71,72](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib72) []](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib71)和图领域[[](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib19) [43,19](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib43) ]中找到，是一个有前途的研究方向。

In the realm of vision, Visual Foundation Models (VFMs) have gained significant success, making substantial impacts on areas such as image recognition, object detection, and scene understanding. Specifically, VFMs benefit from pre-training on extensive and diverse image datasets, allowing them to learn intricate patterns and features. For instance, models such as DALL-E [[73](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib73)], and CLIP [[71](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib71)] leverage self-supervised learning to understand and generate images based on textual descriptions, demonstrating remarkable cross-modal understanding capabilities. Recent Visual ChatGPT [[72](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib72)] integrates ChatGPT with a series of Visual Foundation Models (VFMs), making it perform a variety of complex visual tasks. These VFMs allow models to learn from a broader range of visual data, thereby improving their generalizability and robustness.  
在视觉领域，视觉基础模型（VFM）取得了巨大的成功，对图像识别、物体检测和场景理解等领域产生了重大影响。具体来说，VFM 受益于对广泛且多样化的图像数据集的预训练，使它们能够学习复杂的模式和特征。例如，DALL-E [ [73](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib73) ]和CLIP [ [71](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib71) ]等模型利用自我监督学习来理解和生成基于文本描述的图像，展示了卓越的跨模态理解能力。最近的Visual ChatGPT [ [72](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib72) ]将ChatGPT与一系列视觉基础模型（VFM）集成，使其能够执行各种复杂的视觉任务。这些 VFM 允许模型从更广泛的视觉数据中学习，从而提高其通用性和鲁棒性。

In the sphere of Natural Language Processing (NLP), Large Language Models (LLMs) such as ChatGPT and LLaMA have also revolutionized the field [[74](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib74)]. Characterized by their extensive scale, LLMs are trained on billions of parameters using extensive textual datasets, which enable them to excel in comprehending and generating natural language. The landscape of pre-trained language models is diverse, such as GPT (Generative Pre-trained Transformer) [[14](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib14)], BERT (Bidirectional Encoder Representations from Transformers) [[15](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib15)] and T5 (Text-To-Text Transfer Transformer) [[25](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib25)]. These models can broadly fall into three categories: encoder-only, decoder-only, and encoder-decoder models. Encoder-only models, such as BERT, specialize in understanding and interpreting language. In contrast, decoder-only models like GPT excel in generating coherent and contextually relevant text. Encoder-decoder models, like T5, combine both abilities, efficiently performing various NLP tasks from translation to summarization.  
在自然语言处理（NLP）领域，ChatGPT 和 LLaMA 等大型语言模型（ LLMs ）也彻底改变了该领域[ [74](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib74) ] 。 LLMs的特点是规模庞大，使用广泛的文本数据集对数十亿个参数进行训练，这使他们能够擅长理解和生成自然语言。预训练语言模型的前景多种多样，例如 GPT（生成式预训练变压器） [ [14](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib14) ] 、BERT（来自变压器的双向编码器表示） [ [15](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib15) ]和 T5（文本到文本传输变压器） [ [25](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib25) ] 。这些模型大致可分为三类：仅编码器模型、仅解码器模型和编码器-解码器模型。仅编码器模型，例如 BERT，专门用于理解和解释语言。相比之下，像 GPT 这样的纯解码器模型在生成连贯且上下文相关的文本方面表现出色。编码器-解码器模型（如 T5）结合了这两种能力，有效地执行从翻译到摘要的各种 NLP 任务。

As an encoder-only model, BERT introduces a paradigm in NLP with its innovative bi-directional attention mechanism, which analyzes text from both directions simultaneously, unlike its predecessors like transformer which processed text in a single direction (either left-to-right or right-to-left). This feature allows BERT to attain a comprehensive context understanding, significantly improving its language nuance comprehension. On the other hand, decoder-only models such as GPT, including variants like ChatGPT, utilize a unidirectional self-attention mechanism. This design makes them particularly effective in predicting subsequent words in a sequence, thus excelling in tasks like text completion, creative writing, language translation, and code generation [[75](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib75)]. Additionally, as an encoder-decoder model, T5 uniquely transforms a variety of NLP tasks as text generation problems. For example, it reframes sentiment analysis from a classification task to a text generation task, where input like ”Sentiment: Today is sunny” would prompt T5 to generate an output such as ”Positive”. This text-to-text approach underscores T5’s versatility and adaptability across diverse language tasks.  
作为仅编码器模型，BERT 以其创新的双向注意力机制引入了 NLP 范式，该机制可以同时分析两个方向的文本，这与 Transformer 等单向（从左到右或从左到右）处理文本的前辈不同。从右到左）。这一特性使 BERT 能够获得全面的上下文理解，显着提高其语言细微差别的理解力。另一方面，GPT 等仅解码器模型（包括 ChatGPT 等变体）利用单向自注意力机制。这种设计使它们在预测序列中的后续单词方面特别有效，从而在文本完成、创意写作、语言翻译和代码生成等任务中表现出色[ [75](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib75) ] 。此外，作为编码器-解码器模型，T5 独特地将各种 NLP 任务转化为文本生成问题。例如，它将情感分析从分类任务重新构建为文本生成任务，其中“情感：今天天气晴朗”等输入将提示 T5 生成“积极”等输出。这种文本到文本的方法强调了 T5 在不同语言任务中的多功能性和适应性。
