|DeepGPT [[96](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib96)]  <br>深GPT [ [96](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib96) ]|Graph Transformer 图转换器|Graph Regression 图回归|Prompt Tuning 及时调整|Graph 图形|

The evolution of LLMs has seen the emergence of advanced models like GPT-3 [[97](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib97)], LaMDA [[98](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib98)], PaLM [[99](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib99)], and Vicuna [[68](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib68)]. These models represent significant advances in NLP, distinguished by their enhanced capabilities in comprehending and generating complex, fine-grained language. Their training methods are usually more sophisticated, involving larger datasets and more powerful computational resources. This scaling up has led to unprecedented language understanding and generation capabilities, exhibiting emergent properties such as in-context learning (ICL), adaptability, and flexibility. Furthermore, recent advancements demonstrate the successful integration of LLMs with other models, like recommender system [[17](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib17)], reinforcement learning (RL) [[100](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib100)], GNNs [[101](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib101), [26](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib26), [102](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib102), [103](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib103)]. This integration enables LLMs to tackle both traditional and novel challenges, proposing prospective avenues for applications.  
LLMs的发展见证了先进模型的出现，如 GPT-3 [ [97](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib97) ] 、LaMDA [ [98](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib98) ] 、PaLM [ [99](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib99) ]和 Vicuna [ [68](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib68) ] 。这些模型代表了 NLP 的重大进步，其特点是理解和生成复杂、细粒度语言的能力增强。他们的训练方法通常更复杂，涉及更大的数据集和更强大的计算资源。这种扩展带来了前所未有的语言理解和生成能力，表现出诸如上下文学习（ICL）、适应性和灵活性等新兴特性。此外，最近的进展证明了LLMs与其他模型的成功集成，例如推荐系统[ [17](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib17) ] 、强化学习 (RL) [ [100](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib100) ] 、GNN [[](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib102) [101、26、102、103](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib26) []](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib103) [。](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib101)这种整合使LLMs能够应对传统和新的挑战，为应用提出潜在的途径。

LLMs have found applications in diverse sectors like chemistry [[104](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib104), [105](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib105)], education [[106](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib106), [107](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib107)], and finance [[108](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib108), [109](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib109)]. In these fields, they contribute to various tasks from data analysis to personalized learning. Particularly, LLMs exhibit great potential in graph tasks such as graph classification and link prediction, demonstrating their versatility and broad applicability. Specifically, several studies like Simteg [[26](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib26)], GraD [[102](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib102)], Graph-Toolformer [[101](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib101)], Graph CoT [[110](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib110)], and Graphologue [[103](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib103)] have notably advanced graph learning. These models utilize LLMs for textual graph learning, graph-aware distillation, and graph reasoning, illustrating the potential of LLMs in enhancing the understanding of and interaction with complex graph structures.  
LLMs已在化学[ [104](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib104) , [105](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib105) ] 、教育[ [106](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib106) , [107](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib107) ]和金融[ [108](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib108) , [109](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib109) ]等不同领域得到应用。在这些领域，他们为从数据分析到个性化学习的各种任务做出了贡献。特别是， LLMs在图分类和链接预测等图任务中表现出巨大的潜力，展示了其多功能性和广泛的适用性。具体来说，Simteg [ [26](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib26) ] 、GraD [ [102](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib102) ] 、Graph-Toolformer [ [101](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib101) ] 、Graph CoT [ [110](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib110) ]和 Graphologue [ [103](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib103) ]等多项研究在图学习方面取得了显着的进展。这些模型利用LLMs进行文本图学习、图感知蒸馏和图推理，说明了LLMs在增强对复杂图结构的理解和交互方面的潜力。

Although FMs have revolutionized Vision and NLP domains, the development of Graph Foundation Models (GFMs) is still in the nascent stages. With the rapid evolution and significant potential of this field, it is imperative to continue exploring and developing advanced techniques that can further enhance Graph ML towards GFMs.  
尽管 FM 彻底改变了视觉和 NLP 领域，但图基础模型（GFM）的发展仍处于初级阶段。随着该领域的快速发展和巨大潜力，必须继续探索和开发先进技术，以进一步增强 Graph ML 向 GFM 的发展。


#### 3.2.1Graph Pretext Tasks  
3.2.1图借口任务

Graph Contrastive Learning aims to learn augmentation representations by contrasting similar and dissimilar graph data pairs, effectively identifying nuanced relationships and structural patterns. We can review graph contrastive learning from two perspectives: graph augmentations and the scale of contrast.  
图对比学习旨在通过对比相似和不相似的图数据对来学习增强表示，有效识别细微的关系和结构模式。我们可以从两个角度回顾图对比学习：图增强和对比尺度。

Generally, graph augmentations can be broadly categorized into two types: 1) _feature perturbation_ and 2) _topology perturbation_. They assume that tiny changes in the feature or structural space do not change the semantics of the Node/Edge/(sub)graph. Feature perturbation involves perturbing the features of the nodes in the graph. For example, GRACE [[77](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib77)] randomly masks the node features to learn more robust representations. On the other hand, topology perturbation mainly involves modifying the structure of the graph. A typical example is CSSL [[11](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib11)] which employs strategies like edge perturbation or node dropping to adopt graph-graph level contrast, thereby enhancing the robustness of representations.  
一般来说，图增强可以大致分为两种类型：1）_特征扰动_和2）_拓扑扰动_。他们假设特征或结构空间的微小变化不会改变节点/边/（子）图的语义。特征扰动涉及扰动图中节点的特征。例如，GRACE [ [77](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib77) ]随机屏蔽节点特征以学习更稳健的表示。另一方面，拓扑扰动主要涉及修改图的结构。一个典型的例子是CSSL [ [11](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib11) ]，它采用边缘扰动或节点丢弃等策略来采用图-图级别的对比，从而增强表示的鲁棒性。

Regarding the scale of contrast, the approaches can be divided into node-level and graph-level. For example, GRACE [[77](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib77)] computes the similarities between node-level embeddings to learn discriminative node representations. GCC [[13](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib13)] also works at the node level but learns local structural patterns by sampling a node’s neighbors to obtain subgraphs (positive pairs) and contrasting them with randomly selected non-contextual subgraphs (negative pairs). In contrast, DGI [[76](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib76)] contrasts node-level embeddings with graph-level embedding to capture global graph structures. GraphCL [[10](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib10)] takes a different approach by implementing graph-to-graph level contrast, thereby learning robust representations. The scale used for pre-training has a huge impact on the downstream performance. When adopting contrastive learning as the pre-training task, one key challenge is how to design the objective such that the embeddings learned can account for downstream tasks of different scales.  
根据对比的规模，这些方法可以分为节点级和图级。例如，GRACE [ [77](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib77) ]计算​​节点级嵌入之间的相似性以学习判别性节点表示。 GCC [ [13](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib13) ]也在节点级别工作，但通过对节点的邻居进行采样以获得子图（正对）并将它们与随机选择的非上下文子图（负对）进行对比来学习局部结构模式。相反，DGI [ [76](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib76) ]将节点级嵌入与图级嵌入进行对比，以捕获全局图结构。 GraphCL [ [10](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib10) ]采用不同的方法，通过实现图到图级别的对比，从而学习鲁棒的表示。用于预训练的规模对下游性能有巨大影响。当采用对比学习作为预训练任务时，一个关键的挑战是如何设计目标，使得学习到的嵌入能够解释不同规模的下游任务。

Graph Generation methods aim to learn the distribution of graph data to enable graph generation or reconstruction. In contrast to models in CV that predict masked image patches, or in NLP that predict the next token in a sequence, graph data presents a unique challenge due to its interconnected nature. Consequently, graph generation methods typically work on the feature or structural space. Feature generation methods focus on masking the features of one or a subset of nodes and then training the model to recover the masked features. For instance, GraphMAE [[78](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib78)] utilizes a masked autoencoder framework to reconstruct masked graph portions based on their context, effectively capturing the underlying node semantics and their connection patterns. Alternatively, structure generation methods concentrate on training the model to recover the graph structure. The method GraphGPT [[84](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib84)] encodes the graph into sequences of tokens and then employs a transformer decoder to predict the next token of the sequence to recover the connectivity of the graph. In addition, Graph-Bert [[60](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib60)] is trained on both node attribute recovery and graph structure recovery tasks to ensure that the model captures local node attribute information while maintaining a global view of the graph structure.  
图生成方法旨在学习图数据的分布，以实现图生成或重建。与 CV 中预测屏蔽图像块的模型或 NLP 中预测序列中下一个标记的模型相比，图数据由于其相互关联的性质而提出了独特的挑战。因此，图生成方法通常适用于特征或结构空间。特征生成方法侧重于屏蔽一个或节点子集的特征，然后训练模型以恢复屏蔽的特征。例如，GraphMAE [ [78](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib78) ]利用屏蔽自动编码器框架根据上下文重建屏蔽图部分，有效捕获底层节点语义及其连接模式。或者，结构生成方法集中于训练模型以恢复图结构。 GraphGPT [ [84](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib84) ]方法将图编码为标记序列，然后使用转换器解码器来预测序列的下一个标记以恢复图的连接性。此外，Graph-Bert [ [60](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib60) ]在节点属性恢复和图结构恢复任务上进行了训练，以确保模型捕获本地节点属性信息，同时保持图结构的全局视图。

Graph Property Prediction methods gain guidance from the node-, edge-, and graph-level properties, which are inherently present in the graph data. These methods follow a training approach similar to supervised learning, as both utilize ”sample-label” pairs for training. The key distinction lies in the origin of the labels: in supervised learning, labels are manually annotated by human experts which can be costly in real scenarios, whereas in property-based learning, the labels are automatically generated from the graph using some heuristics or algorithms. For example, GROVER [[82](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib82)] utilizes professional software to extract the information on graph motifs as labels for classification. Similarly,  [[119](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib119)] leverage statistical properties of the graph for graph self-supervised learning.  
图属性预测方法从节点、边缘和图级属性中获得指导，这些属性固有地存在于图数据中。这些方法遵循类似于监督学习的训练方法，因为两者都利用“样本-标签”对进行训练。关键区别在于标签的来源：在监督学习中，标签由人类专家手动注释，这在实际场景中可能成本高昂，而在基于属性的学习中，标签是使用一些启发式或算法从图中自动生成的。例如，GROVER [ [82](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib82) ]利用专业软件提取图形主题的信息作为分类标签。类似地， [ [119](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib119) ]利用图的统计特性进行图自监督学习。

#### 3.2.2Downstream Adaptation  
3.2.2下游适配

Unsupervised Representation Learning (URL) is a common method due to the scarcity of labeled data in the real world [[76](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib76), [77](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib77), [78](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib78), [79](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib79)]. In URL, the pre-trained graph encoder is frozen and only a task-specific layer is learned during downstream tuning. The learned representations are then directly fed into decoders. This pattern allows URLs to be efficiently applied to downstream tasks. For example, DGI [[76](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib76)] trains an encoder model to learn node representations within graph-structured. Node representations can then be used for downstream tasks. However, due to the gap between the pretext task and downstream tasks, URL can also lead to suboptimal performance.  
由于现实世界中标记数据的稀缺性，无监督表示学习（URL）是一种常用的方法[[](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib79) [76,77,78,79](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib77) []](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib78) [。](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib76)在 URL 中，预训练的图形编码器被冻结，并且在下游调整期间仅学习特定于任务的层。然后将学习到的表示直接输入解码器。此模式允许 URL 有效地应用于下游任务。例如，DGI [ [76](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib76) ]训练编码器模型来学习图结构内的节点表示。然后，节点表示可用于下游任务。然而，由于前置任务和下游任务之间的差距，URL 也会导致性能不佳。

Fine-tuning is the default method to adapt a pre-trained model to a certain downstream task. As shown in Figure [3](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#S3.F3 "Figure 3 ‣ 3.1.2 Graph Transformer-based Model ‣ 3.1 Backbone Architecture ‣ 3 Deep Learning on Graphs ‣ Graph Machine Learning in the Era of Large Language Models (LLMs)"), it adds a randomly initialized task header (e.g., a classifier) on top of the pre-trained model, and during fine-tuning, both the backbone model and the header are jointly trained [[60](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib60), [10](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib10), [11](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib11)]. Compared with URL, fine-tuning provides more flexibility as it allows changes in the backbone parameters, and one can choose the layers to be tuned while keeping others fixed. Additionally, recent studies [[81](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib81), [83](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib83), [10](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib10)] further explore advanced graph fine-tuning methods that go beyond naive fine-tuning. For instance, AdapterGNN [[81](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib81)] introduces two trainable adapters in parallel before and after the message passing. It freezes the GNN model during fine-tuning while only tuning the adapters, enabling parameter-efficient fine-tuning with minimal influence on the downstream performance.  
微调是使预训练模型适应特定下游任务的默认方法。如图[3](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#S3.F3 "Figure 3 ‣ 3.1.2 Graph Transformer-based Model ‣ 3.1 Backbone Architecture ‣ 3 Deep Learning on Graphs ‣ Graph Machine Learning in the Era of Large Language Models (LLMs)")所示，它在预训练模型之上添加了一个随机初始化的任务标头（例如分类器），并且在微调期间，骨干模型和标头都被联合训练[[](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib10) [60,10,11](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib60) []](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib11) ] 。与 URL 相比，微调提供了更大的灵活性，因为它允许更改主干参数，并且可以选择要调整的层，同时保持其他层固定。此外，最近的研究[[](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib10) [81,83,10](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib81) []](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib83)进一步探索了超越简单微调的高级图微调方法。例如，AdapterGNN [ [81](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib81) ]在消息传递之前和之后并行引入了两个可训练的适配器。它在微调期间冻结 GNN 模型，而仅调整适配器，从而实现参数高效的微调，同时对下游性能的影响最小。

Prompt-tuning: ”Pre-training & fine-tuning” is prevalent in adapting pre-trained models to specific downstream tasks, but it overlooks the gap between pre-training and downstream tasks, potentially limiting generalization capabilities. Moreover, fine-tuning for different tasks also leads to significant time and computational costs. Inspired by recent advancements in NLP, several methods [[87](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib87), [95](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib95), [88](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib88), [91](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib91), [89](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib89), [90](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib90), [93](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib93), [92](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib92), [96](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib96)] have presented the potential of introducing prompts to adapt pre-trained models to specific tasks as illustrated in Figure [3](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#S3.F3 "Figure 3 ‣ 3.1.2 Graph Transformer-based Model ‣ 3.1 Backbone Architecture ‣ 3 Deep Learning on Graphs ‣ Graph Machine Learning in the Era of Large Language Models (LLMs)"). Specifically, Prompt-tuning first unifies the downstream task with the pre-trained task into the same paradigm, followed by the introduction of learnable prompts for tuning. For example, GPPT [[88](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib88)] first reframe node classification as link predictions. GraphPrompt [[87](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib87)] further extends graph classification into link prediction. On the other hand, Prog [[91](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib91)] unifies all the downstream tasks into subgraph classification. The inserting prompt including vectors [[88](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib88), [87](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib87), [90](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib90)], node [[95](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib95)] and sub-graph [[91](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib91)]. By inserting these prompts, the pre-trained parameters can be utilized in a way that aligns more closely with the requirements of the downstream tasks.  
及时调整： “预训练和微调”在使预训练模型适应特定下游任务方面很普遍，但它忽略了预训练和下游任务之间的差距，可能限制泛化能力。此外，针对不同任务的微调也会导致大量的时间和计算成本。受 NLP 最新[进展](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib89)[的](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib90)[启发](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib87)[，](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib95)[多种](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib96)[方法](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib92)[[](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib88) [87、95、88、91、89、90、93、92、96](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib93) []](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib91)展现了引入提示以使预训练模型适应特定任务的潜力，如图[3](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#S3.F3 "Figure 3 ‣ 3.1.2 Graph Transformer-based Model ‣ 3.1 Backbone Architecture ‣ 3 Deep Learning on Graphs ‣ Graph Machine Learning in the Era of Large Language Models (LLMs)")所示。具体来说，提示调优首先将下游任务与预训练任务统一到同一范式中，然后引入可学习的调优提示。例如，GPPT [ [88](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib88) ]首先将节点分类重新构建为链接预测。 GraphPrompt [ [87](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib87) ]进一步将图分类扩展到链接预测。另一方面，Prog [ [91](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib91) ]将所有下游任务统一为子图分类。插入提示包括向量[[](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib88) [88,87,90](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib90) []](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib87) ，节点[ [95](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib95) ]和子图[ [91](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib91) ] 。通过插入这些提示，可以以更符合下游任务要求的方式利用预训练参数。

![Refer to caption](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2/x4.png)

Figure 4:Illustration of LLMs for Graph ML. (1) Methods using LLMs for Enhancing Feature Quality by enhancing feature representation, generating augmented information, and aligning feature space. (2) Explorations for solving Vanilla GNN Training Limitations are categorized based on how structural information in the graph is processed: ignoring structural information, implicit structural information, and explicit structural information. (3) Research about employing LLMs to alleviate the limitations of Heterophily and Generalization.  
图 4：图 ML 的LLMs插图。 (1) 使用LLMs通过增强特征表示、生成增强信息和对齐特征空间来增强特征质量的方法。 (2)解决 Vanilla GNN 训练限制的探索根据图中结构信息的处理方式进行分类：忽略结构信息、隐式结构信息和显式结构信息。 (3)利用LLMs缓解异质性和泛化性局限性的研究。


## 7Future Directions  
7未来方向

In this survey, we have thoroughly reviewed the latest developments of Graph Machine Learning in the era of LLMs, revealing significant advancements and potential in this field. By harnessing the power of LLMs, it is potential to enhance Graph ML to enable GFMs. As this research direction is still in the exploratory stage, future directions in this field can be diverse and innovative. Therefore, in this section, we delve into several potential future directions of this promising field.  
在本次调查中，我们全面回顾了LLMs时代图机器学习的最新发展，揭示了该领域的重大进展和潜力。通过利用LLMs的力量，有可能增强 Graph ML 以实现 GFM。由于该研究方向仍处于探索阶段，未来该领域的方向可以是多元化和创新的。因此，在本节中，我们将深入研究这个有前途的领域的几个潜在的未来方向。

### 7.1Generalization and Transferability  
7.1泛化和可移植性

While Graph ML has deployed for various graph tasks, a notable problem is their limited capacity for generalization and transferability across different graph domains [[40](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib40)]. Different from fields such as NLP and CV, where data often adhere to a uniform format (e.g., a sequence of tokens or a grid of pixels), graphs can be highly heterogeneous in nature. This heterogeneity manifests in varying graph sizes, densities, and types of nodes and edges, which presents a significant challenge in developing a universal model capable of performing optimally across various graph structure data. Currently, LLMs have demonstrated great potentials in improving the generalization ability of the graph model. For example, OFA [[129](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib129)] provides a solution for classification tasks across several certain domains. Nevertheless, there is still scarce exploration of the generalizability of GFMs compared to LLMs. Therefore, future research should aim to develop more adaptable and flexible models that can effectively apply learned patterns from one graph type, such as social networks, to another, like molecular structures, without extensive retraining.  
虽然 Graph ML 已部署用于各种图形任务，但一个值得注意的问题是它们跨不同图形域的泛化和可转移性的能力有限[ [40](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib40) ] 。与 NLP 和 CV 等领域的数据通常遵循统一的格式（例如，令牌序列或像素网格）不同，图本质上可以是高度异构的。这种异质性表现在不同的图大小、密度以及节点和边的类型上，这对开发能够在各种图结构数据上实现最佳性能的通用模型提出了重大挑战。目前， LLMs在提高图模型的泛化能力方面表现出了巨大的潜力。例如，OFA [ [129](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib129) ]为跨多个特定领域的分类任务提供了解决方案。尽管如此，与LLMs相比，GFM 的普遍性仍然缺乏探索。因此，未来的研究应该致力于开发适应性更强、更灵活的模型，能够有效地将学习到的模式从一种图类型（例如社交网络）应用到另一种图类型（例如分子结构），而无需进行大量的再训练。

### 7.2Multi-modal Graph Learning  
7.2多模态图学习

Recent LLMs have shown significant potential in advancing GFMs. Many efforts have been made to transform graph data into formats suitable for LLM input, such as tokens or text [[84](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib84), [27](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib27), [131](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib131)]. However, many nodes in graphs are enriched with diverse modalities of information, including text, images, and videos. Understanding this multi-modal data can potentially benefit graph learning. For example, on social media platforms, a user’s post could include textual content, images, and videos, all of which are valuable for comprehensive user modeling. Given the importance of multi-modal data, a promising direction for future research is to empower LLMs to process and integrate graph structure with multi-modal data. Currently, TOUCHUP-G [[86](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib86)] makes an initial exploration of multi-modal ( i.e., texts, images) in graph learning. In the future, we expect the development of a unified model capable of modeling universal modalities for more advanced GFMs.  
最近的LLMs在推进 GFM 方面表现出了巨大的潜力。为了将图数据转换为适合LLM输入的格式，例如标记或文本[[](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib131) [84,27,131](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib84) ] [，](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib27)人们做出了许多努力。然而，图中的许多节点都富含不同形式的信息，包括文本、图像和视频。理解这种多模态数据可能有利于图学习。例如，在社交媒体平台上，用户的帖子可能包括文本内容、图像和视频，所有这些对于全面的用户建模都很有价值。鉴于多模态数据的重要性，未来研究的一个有希望的方向是使LLMs能够处理并将图结构与多模态数据集成。目前，TOUCHUP-G [ [86](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib86) ]对图学习中的多模态（即文本、图像）进行了初步探索。未来，我们期望开发一个能够为更先进的 GFM 的通用模式建模的统一模型。

### 7.3Trustworthiness  
7.3可信度

The recent applications of LLMs for Graph ML have significantly enhanced graph modeling capabilities and broadened their utility in various fields. Despite these advancements, with the growing reliance on these models, it is important to ensure their trustworthiness, particularly in critical areas like healthcare, finance, and social network analysis [[224](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib224), [225](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib225)]. Robustness is fundamental in safeguarding the models against adversarial attacks, ensuring consistent reliability. Explainability is essential for users to understand and trust the decisions made by these models. Fairness is crucial for the model’s ethical and effective use in various applications. Privacy is important for legal compliance and key to maintaining user trust. Therefore, the development of trustworthy LLMs on graphs must be equipped with _Robustness_&_Safety_, _Explainability_, _Fairness_, and _Privacy_, ensuring their safe and effective use in various applications.  
最近，图机器学习法学LLMs的应用显着增强了图建模能力，并扩大了其在各个领域的实用性。尽管取得了这些进步，但随着对这些模型的依赖日益增加，确保它们的可信度非常重要，特别是在医疗保健、金融和社交网络分析等关键领域[ [224](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib224) , [225](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib225) ] 。鲁棒性是保护模型免受对抗性攻击、确保一致可靠性的基础。可解释性对于用户理解和信任这些模型做出的决策至关重要。公平性对于模型在各种应用中的道德和有效使用至关重要。隐私对于法律合规性非常重要，也是维持用户信任的关键。因此，在图上开发值得信赖的LLMs必须具备_鲁棒性_和_安全性_、_可解释性_、_公平性_和_隐私性_，确保其在各种应用中安全有效地使用。

#### 7.3.1Robustness&Safety  
7.3.1稳健性和安全性

Recently, integrating LLMs into Graph ML has shown promising performance in various downstream tasks, but they are also highly vulnerable to adversarial perturbations, raising significant concerns about their robustness and safety. To enhance the resilience of these models, some studies add adversarial perturbations to GNNs [[226](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib226), [227](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib227)] or LLMs [[228](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib228), [229](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib229)] for adversarial training. However, these methods may not be effective for the new paradigm of Graph ML integrating LLMs, as vulnerabilities can arise from both graphs, such as graph poisoning attacks [[230](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib230), [231](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib231)] and graph modification attacks [[232](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib232), [233](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib233)], and from the language model, like prompt attacks [[234](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib234)] and misleading text data [[235](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib235)]. To address these issues, more sophisticated detection and defense mechanisms need to be developed by considering both the intricacies of LLMs and graphs to ensure the comprehensive safety and robustness of Graph ML.  
最近，将LLMs集成到 Graph ML 中已经在各种下游任务中表现出了良好的性能，但它们也很容易受到对抗性扰动，引发了人们对其鲁棒性和安全性的严重担忧。为了增强这些模型的弹性，一些研究向 GNN [ [226](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib226) , [227](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib227) ]或LLMs [ [228](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib228) , [229](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib229) ]添加对抗性扰动以进行对抗性训练。然而，这些方法对于集成LLMs的图 ML 的新范例可能并不有效，因为两个图都可能产生漏洞，例如图中毒攻击[ [230](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib230) , [231](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib231) ]和图修改攻击[ [232](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib232) , [233](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib233) ] ，以及语言模型，例如提示攻击[ [234](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib234) ]和误导性文本数据[ [235](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib235) ] 。为了解决这些问题，需要通过考虑LLMs和图的复杂性来开发更复杂的检测和防御机制，以确保Graph ML的全面安全性和鲁棒性。

#### 7.3.2Explainability  
7.3.2可解释性

Nowadays, LLMs are increasingly employed in Graph ML across various applications, such as recommender systems [[236](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib236), [15](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib15)] and molecular discovery [[139](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib139), [85](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib85)]. However, due to privacy and security concerns, an application provider may prefer to provide an API version without revealing the architecture and parameters of the LLM, such as with ChatGPT. This lack of transparency can make it challenging for users to understand the model’s results, leading to confusion and dissatisfaction. Therefore, it’s important to enhance the explainability of Graph ML, especially with LLMs. Owing to their reasoning and interpretive capabilities, LLMs are promising to provide better explainability in graph-related tasks. For example, P5 [[236](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib236)] can provide reasons for its recommendations in recommendation tasks. Future efforts should be directed toward making the inner workings of these models more transparent and explainable to better comprehend their decision-making processes.  
如今， LLMs越来越多地应用于图机器学习的各种应用中，例如推荐系统[ [236](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib236) , [15](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib15) ]和分子发现[ [139](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib139) , [85](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib85) ] 。然而，出于隐私和安全考虑，应用程序提供商可能更愿意提供 API 版本而不透露LLM的架构和参数，例如使用 ChatGPT。缺乏透明度可能使用户难以理解模型的结果，从而导致混乱和不满。因此，增强 Graph ML 的可解释性非常重要，尤其是对于LLMs 。由于其推理和解释能力， LLMs有望在图形相关任务中提供更好的可解释性。例如，P5 [ [236](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib236) ]可以在推荐任务中提供其推荐的理由。未来的努力应该致力于使这些模型的内部运作更加透明和可解释，以便更好地理解它们的决策过程。

#### 7.3.3Fairness  
7.3.3公平性

As LLMs become prevalent in enhancing Graph ML towards GFMs, concerns about their fairness are growing. Fairness is crucial to ensure these models operate without biases or discrimination, especially when dealing with complex, interconnected graph data [[225](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib225)]. Recent studies demonstrate that both language models [[237](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib237), [238](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib238)] and GNN models [[239](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib239)] can potentially be discriminatory and unfair [[42](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib42)]. Therefore, it is necessary to maintain fairness in both textual and graph contexts. To enhance the fairness of LLMs, recent studies include retraining strategies that adjust model parameters for unbiased outputs[[240](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib240)], implementing alignment constraints [[241](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib241)], and adopting contrastive learning to diminish bias in model training [[242](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib242)]. Concurrently, studies like FairNeg [[239](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib239)] also explore improving the fairness of recommendation data. Despite these efforts, achieving fairness in GFMs is still a significant challenge that needs further exploration.  
随着LLMs在增强 Graph ML 向 GFM 方面的应用越来越普遍，人们对其公平性的担忧也与日俱增。公平性对于确保这些模型在没有偏见或歧视的情况下运行至关重要，特别是在处理复杂、相互关联的图形数据时[ [225](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib225) ] 。最近的研究表明，语言模型[ [237](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib237) , [238](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib238) ]和 GNN 模型[ [239](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib239) ]都可能具有歧视性和不公平性[ [42](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib42) ] 。因此，有必要在文本和图形上下文中保持公平性。为了提高LLMs的公平性，最近的研究包括调整模型参数以获得无偏输出的再训练策略[ [240](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib240) ] 、实施对齐约束[ [241](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib241) ]以及采用对比学习来减少模型训练中的偏差[ [242](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib242) ] 。同时，像 FairNeg [ [239](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib239) ]这样的研究也探索提高推荐数据的公平性。尽管做出了这些努力，实现 GFM 的公平性仍然是一个重大挑战，需要进一步探索。

#### 7.3.4Privacy  
7.3.4隐私

Privacy is a critical issue in Graph ML, particularly given the risk of these models inadvertently leaking sensitive information contained in graph data [[243](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib243), [244](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib244), [245](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib245)]. For example, Graph ML integrated with LLMs could potentially expose private user data, like browsing histories or social connections when generating outputs. This concern is especially pressing in highly data-sensitive areas such as healthcare or finance. To mitigate these privacy risks,  [[246](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib246)] introduces Privacy-Preserving Prompt Tuning (RAPT) to protect user privacy through local differential privacy. Future exploration in LLM-enhanced Graph ML should also focus on integrating privacy-preserving technologies like differential privacy and federated learning to strengthen data security and user privacy.  
隐私是图机器学习中的一个关键问题，特别是考虑到这些模型无意中泄露图数据中包含的敏感信息的风险[[](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib244) [243,244,245](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib245) []](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib243) 。例如，与LLMs集成的 Graph ML 可能会暴露私人用户数据，例如生成输出时的浏览历史或社交关系。这种担忧在医疗保健或金融等数据高度敏感的领域尤其紧迫。为了减轻这些隐私风险， [ [246](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib246) ]引入了隐私保护提示调整（RAPT）来通过本地差分隐私来保护用户隐私。 LLM增强图 ML 的未来探索还应侧重于集成隐私保护技术，如差分隐私和联邦学习，以加强数据安全和用户隐私。

### 7.4Efficiency  
7.4效率

While LLMs have proven effective in constructing GFMs, their operational efficiency, particularly in processing large and complex graphs, is still a significant challenge [[247](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib247)]. For example, the use of APIs like GPT4 for large-scale graph tasks can lead to high costs under current billing models. Additionally, deploying open-source large models (e.g., LLaMa) for parameter updates or just inference in local environments demands substantial computational resources and storage. Therefore, enhancing the efficiency of LLMs for graph tasks remains a critical issue. Recent studies introduce techniques like LoRA [[156](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib156)] and QLoRA [[248](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib248)] to fine-tune LLM parameters more efficiently. Furthermore, model pruning [[249](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib249), [250](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib250)] is also a promising method to increase efficiency by removing redundant parameters or structures from LLMs, thereby simplifying their application in graph machine learning.  
虽然LLMs已被证明在构建 GFM 方面是有效的，但它们的操作效率，特别是在处理大型复杂图时，仍然是一个重大挑战[ [247](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib247) ] 。例如，使用 GPT4 等 API 进行大规模图形任务可能会导致当前计费模型下的高成本。此外，部署开源大型模型（例如 LLaMa）以进行参数更新或仅在本地环境中进行推理需要大量的计算资源和存储。因此，提高LLMs在图任务上的效率仍然是一个关键问题。最近的研究引入了 LoRA [ [156](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib156) ]和 QLoRA [ [248](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib248) ]等技术来更有效地微调LLM参数。此外，模型剪枝[ [249](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib249) , [250](https://arxiv.org/html/2404.14928v2#bib.bib250) ]也是一种有前途的方法，通过从LLMs​​中删除冗余参数或结构来提高效率，从而简化它们在图机器学习中的应用。



#    An Opinion Diffusion Model with Vigilant Agents and Deliberation   具有警惕代理人和深思熟虑的意见扩散模型
https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7
### 3.1 Making Sense of the Opinion Dynamics with Epistemic Vigilant Agents  
3.1理解认知警惕主体的观点动态

Thorough observations of the model’s runs in the parameter space from Table [1](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7#Tab1) show that epistemic vigilance plays an important role in the dynamics of opinions. The first observations call for a fine distinction of the dynamics’ steady states. For instance, we consider bipolarity (2 stable clusters), 3-pluriformity and, 4-pluriformity (3 and 4 stable clusters, respectively) as being moderate or extreme (having at least one of the opinion cluster in an extreme position within the opinion domain).  
对表[1](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7#Tab1)中参数空间中模型运行的彻底观察表明，认知警惕在观点动态中发挥着重要作用。第一个观察结果需要对动力学的稳态进行精细区分。例如，我们认为双极性（2个稳定簇）、3-多形性和4-多形性（分别为3和4个稳定簇）为中等或极端（至少有一个意见簇处于意见内的极端位置）领域）。

Table [2](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7#Tab2) summarizes our findings over all runs executed for each of the models. The first interesting result is that epistemic vigilance allows for uniformity and extreme bipolarity to occur, when they barely occur in the reference model. Moreover, the proportional number of cases in which there is bipolarization (especially for extreme bipolarization) is higher for epistemic vigilant agents than for non-epistemic vigilant ones. This is due to the scenarios in which the agents are ego-involved ((U,T)=(0.4,1.6)), are not too demanding in terms of coherence checking (0.5≥V≥0.35), and have sufficiently many arguments to communicate their positions (k≥8). In these scenarios, small extreme opinion clusters form quickly. Agents easily accept the justification arguments they are given since they have a high tolerance to message-source discrepancy and may not have the necessary arguments to avoid being influenced – moderate agents begin to drift towards the extremes of the opinion domain. The result is a steady state with two clusters, one at each end of the opinion domain (see Fig. [3](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7#Fig3)h). Deliberation only amplifies the drift towards the extremes because the agents are only affected by deliberated decisions that are sufficiently close to or far from their opinions. Moreover, they may retrieve stronger justification arguments during group discussion, which makes them more convincing and more prone to repel one another in pair-wise interactions (see Fig. [3](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7#Fig3)i).  
表总结了我们对每个模型执行的所有运行的发现。第一个有趣的结果是，认知警惕性允许一致性和极端双极性的发生，而它们在参考模型中几乎不出现。此外，认知警惕者中存在双极化（尤其是极端双极化）的案例比例高于非认知警惕者。这是由于代理人有自我意识的情况造成的（ (U,T)=(0.4,1.6) ），在一致性检查方面要求不太高（ 0.5≥V≥0.35 ），并且有足够多的论点来表达他们的立场（ k≥8 ）。在这些情况下，小型极端意见集群很快就会形成。代理人很容易接受他们给出的正当理由，因为他们对消息源差异有很高的容忍度，并且可能没有必要的论据来避免受到影响——温和的代理人开始走向意见领域的极端。结果是具有两个簇的稳定状态，每个簇位于意见域的每一端（见图 h）。深思熟虑只会放大走向极端的倾向，因为代理人只会受到与他们的观点足够接近或远离的深思熟虑的决定的影响。此外，他们可能在小组讨论中检索出更有力的论证，这使得他们在成对互动中更有说服力，也更容易相互排斥（见图一）。

**Table 3. Model-to-model differences for the mean values of the observations over all simulations (confidence level of 0.95). Entries in bold indicate a non-significant difference. Ts is computed only for the scenarios in which opinions converge. Values are rounded to the nearest hundredth.**

[Full size table 全尺寸桌子](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7/tables/3)

A second interesting observation is that epistemic vigilance allows for more 4-pluriformity scenarios than the reference model, and it dwindles in n-pluriformity steady states. This comes from the scenarios in which agents are less ego-involved ((U,T)=(0.2,T′), T′≥1.6)), somewhat more demanding in terms of coherence checking (V∈[0.25,0.35]) and have fewer arguments (k≤8). As observed in the transition from Figs. [3](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7#Fig3)a to [3](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7#Fig3)b, interactions that lead to contrast responses are blocked due to epistemic vigilance. Agents have trouble influencing one another. The clusters at the extreme of the opinion domain fail to form, and the handful of extreme-opinionated agents are absorbed into more moderate clusters. Similarly, the transition from Figs. [3](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7#Fig3)d to [3](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7#Fig3)e shows how epistemic vigilance impedes the emergence of a central cluster and yields a 4-pluriformity steady state. One possible explanation is that low epistemic vigilance allows for more social influence to occur than in the reference model. The agents that would end up in the central cluster in Fig. [3](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7#Fig3)d are absorbed into one of the non-neutral moderate clusters, and some agents in the moderate clusters are pushed or attracted to the extreme clusters. As expected for these scenarios, adding deliberation into the dynamics reduces the number of opinion clusters observed throughout the simulations. Deliberative opinion shifts destabilize non-extreme opinion clusters and pave the way for the emergence of new, more moderate clusters as observed in Figs. [3](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7#Fig3)c and [3](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7#Fig3)f. Likewise, deliberation may be responsible for the emergence of extreme clusters, as presented in the transition from Fig. [3](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7#Fig3)b to Fig. [3](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7#Fig3)c.  
第二个有趣的观察是，认知警惕性比参考模型允许更多的 4 多元化场景，并且它在 n 多元化稳定状态下会减少。这来自于代理较少自我参与的场景（ (U,T)=(0.2,T′) , T′≥1.6 ))，在一致性检查方面要求更高一些( V∈[0.25,0.35]) 并且有更少的参数（ k≤8 ）。正如从图 1 和 2 的转变中观察到的那样。 a 到 b，由于认知警惕，导致对比反应的相互作用被阻止。特工们很难相互影响。意见领域极端的集群未能形成，少数极端观点的代理人被吸收到更温和的集群中。类似地，从图1到图2的转变。 d 到 e 显示了认知警惕如何阻碍中心簇的出现并产生 4 多重性稳态。一种可能的解释是，与参考模型相比，认知警惕性较低会产生更多的社会影响。最终进入图 d 中中心集群的智能体被吸收到非中性中等集群之一中，中等集群中的一些智能体被推或吸引到极端集群。正如对这些场景的预期，在动态中添加深思熟虑会减少在整个模拟过程中观察到的意见集群的数量。慎重的意见转变会破坏非极端意见集群的稳定，并为新的、更温和的集群的出现铺平道路，如图 1 和 1 所示。 c和f。同样，深思熟虑可能是极端集群出现的原因，如图 b 到图 c 的过渡所示。

**Comparing the Models Using the Metrics of Interest.** We examine the mean value of each metric over all simulations. We quickly infer that a high variance of opinions is an indicator of the presence of extremists (ρ≈0.95, p<0.001). Thus, we study one or the other interchangeably.  
我们检查所有模拟中每个指标的平均值。我们很快推断，意见分歧很大是极端分子存在的一个指标（ ρ≈0.95 , p<0.001 ）。因此，我们可以互换地研究其中之一。

From Table [3](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7#Tab3), we can say that epistemic vigilance allows for an increase in the variance of opinions compared to the scenario in which agents do not apply epistemic vigilance (reference model). This may be the case because a large number of simulations in the epistemic vigilance model result in an extreme bipolar convergence of opinions. Indeed, opinion bipolarization occurs when the latitude of non-commitment is smaller ((U,T)=(0.4,1.6)) and epistemic vigilance is moderate (k≥8 and V≥0.35). Otherwise, a sundry of different opinion distributions appears (see Fig. [3](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7#Fig3)) for which we can say little about the average variance of opinions over all the simulations. This diversity of steady states could explain why the proportion of convergent simulations for epistemic vigilance agents is smaller than that of the reference model. For the convergent scenarios, however, the model with epistemic vigilant agents is faster to converge. This was unaccounted for and may also be explained by the scenarios in which extreme bipolarization occurs (e.g. Fig. [3](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7#Fig3)h).  
从表中，我们可以说，与主体不应用认知警惕的场景（参考模型）相比，认知警惕会增加意见的方差。情况可能如此，因为认知警惕模型中的大量模拟导致了意见的极端两极趋同。事实上，当不承诺的范围较小时，就会出现意见两极分化（ (U,T)=(0.4,1.6) ）并且认知警惕性中等（ k≥8 和 V≥0.35 ）。否则，就会出现各种不同的意见分布（见图 1），对于所有模拟中意见的平均方差，我们几乎无话可说。这种稳态的多样性可以解释为什么认知警戒主体的收敛模拟比例小于参考模型的比例。然而，对于收敛场景，具有认知警惕代理的模型收敛速度更快。这是无法解释的，也可以通过极端两极分化发生的场景来解释（例如图h）。

**Fig. 4. 图 4.**

[![figure 4](https://media.springernature.com/lw685/springer-static/image/chp%3A10.1007%2F978-3-030-60843-9_7/MediaObjects/505059_1_En_7_Fig4_HTML.png)](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7/figures/4)

Curves of mean observations for the runs on the metrics (0.95 confidence intervals).  
指标运行的平均观测值曲线（0.95 置信区间）。

[Full size image 全尺寸图像](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7/figures/4)

Surprisingly, adding deliberation to the model in which agents are vigilant does not seem to affect the average variance of opinions. Either the number of observations is too small to establish a difference among the two models (skewed confidence interval) or deliberation’s variance increasing effects (e.g. emergence of extremism) cancel out with its variance decreasing effects (e.g. emergence of moderate clusters). Finally, the mean correctness of deliberated decisions is higher when agents deliberate, as compared to the implicit acceptance of all the proposal arguments in the non-deliberative models. The difference is of, on average, 27 incorrect decisions per 100 deliberated issues.  
令人惊讶的是，在代理人保持警惕的模型中添加深思熟虑似乎并没有影响意见的平均方差。要么是观察数量太少，无法在两个模型之间建立差异（倾斜的置信区间），要么是深思熟虑的方差增加效应（例如，极端主义的出现）与其方差减小效应（例如，温和集群的出现）相抵消。最后，与非商议模型中隐式接受所有提案论点相比，当代理人深思熟虑时，深思熟虑决策的平均正确性更高。差异在于，每 100 个深思熟虑的问题平均有 27 个错误决策。

### 3.2 Sensitivity Analysis of Deliberation Parameters  
3.2审议参数的敏感性分析

For the analysis, we fix all the parameters that are not procedural to an intermediate value inspired from their domains: (U,T,V,k)=(0.3,1.7,0.3,8). The varying parameters are those entitled “Deliberation Protocol” in Table [1](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7#Tab1). In the analysis, vI may be generated randomly (the _R_ rule) or computed from a random one-third sample of the population (the _S_ rule). With the _S_ rule, the proposals discussed are, on average, more neutral. Also, the CA may choose to balance (have the same number of agents from both sides of the opinion spectrum) the deliberation table. We do not discuss convergence in the sensitivity analysis since the dynamics rarely converges when there is deliberation.  
为了进行分析，我们将所有非程序参数固定为受其领域启发的中间值： (U,T,V,k)=(0.3,1.7,0.3,8) 。不同的参数是表中标题为“审议协议”的参数。在分析中， vI 可以随机生成（规则）或从总体的随机三分之一样本计算（规则）。根据该规则，所讨论的提案平均而言更加中立。此外，CA 可以选择平衡审议表（意见范围双方的代理人数量相同）。我们不讨论敏感性分析中的收敛，因为在深思熟虑时动态很少收敛。

**Number of Debates (**_m_**).** The number of debates do not have a significant effect on the variance of opinions. We may attribute this to the fact that either the number of agents engaged in deliberation is too small to actually push the dynamics (which is surprising for nD=0.25) or because the long debates may usually end with undecided proposal arguments. What is quite interesting, however, is that the number of debates has a negative marginally decreasing effect on judgment inaccuracy (see Fig. [4](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7#Fig4)c). The jump from 3 to 5 debates has a weak or insignificant positive effect on the quality of the deliberated outcomes. We expected that the effect would vanish when nD was high, but it did even when nD was low (strong substitution effect for the size of deliberation).  
辩论次数对意见分歧没有显着影响。我们可以将其归因于这样一个事实：参与审议的代理人数量太少，无法真正推动动态（这对于 nD=0.25 ）或者因为长时间的辩论通常可能以未定的提案争论结束。然而，非常有趣的是，辩论的数量对判断不准确性有负边际递减的影响（见图c）。从 3 场辩论跃升至 5 场辩论对审议结果的质量产生微弱或微不足道的积极影响。我们预计，当 nD 很高，但即使在 nD 较低（审议规模的替代效应较强）。

**Proportion of the Population in Deliberation Steps (**nD**).** As expected, the more agents participate in the debate, the better it is for the accuracy of the decisions. The effect is marginally decreasing and seems to reach an asymptote at around nD=0.25 for each value of _m_. This means that if 25% of the agents are summoned to the deliberation table, then they are numerous enough to reach a stable and relatively low average level of correctness (Q<0.5). We expected to find a higher statistic since the more agents there are, the easier it is to stumble upon an agent that would give up on a correct labeling to win the debate (see Fig. [4](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7#Fig4)c). This could explain the marginally decreasing effect of nD on _Q_. The variance of opinions over nD varies depending on the rule used to generate vI. A smaller deliberation arena implies a smaller variance of opinion only if the proposals the agents discuss are uniformly and randomly distributed. Randomness in the topic of discussion can lead to discussions on “extreme” topics and either pull (the proposals are accepted) or push (the proposals are rejected) agents to the extremes of the opinion distribution. Due to a small sample and effect size, however, it is difficult to assert the parameter’s influence on opinions (see Fig. [4](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7#Fig4)a).  
nD 正如预期的那样，参与辩论的智能体越多，决策的准确性就越好。效果略有减弱，并且似乎在大约处达到渐近线 nD=0.25 对于 的每个值。这意味着，如果 25% 的智能体被召集到审议表上，那么它们的数量就足以达到稳定且相对较低的平均正确性水平（ Q<0.5 ）。我们期望找到更高的统计数据，因为智能体越多，就越容易发现一个智能体会放弃正确的标签来赢得辩论（见图 c）。这可以解释 nD 在 。各方意见分歧 nD 取决于用于生成的规则而变化 vI 。仅当代理人讨论的提案均匀且随机分布时，较小的审议范围意味着较小的意见分歧。讨论主题的随机性可能会导致对“极端”主题的讨论，并将代理人拉（提案被接受）或推（提案被拒绝）到意见分布的极端。然而，由于样本和效应量较小，很难断言参数对意见的影响（见图a）。

## 4 Related Work  
4相关工作

Most models in the literature of opinion diffusion are interested in opinions because these have an influence on collective decision-making and on matters of social order. For instance, authors in [[10](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7#ref-CR10 "Galam, S., Moscovici, S.: Towards a theory of collective phenomena: consensus and attitude changes in groups. Eur. J. Soc. Psychol. 21(1), 49–74 (1991)")] are interested in consensus formation and in how groups choose between two alternatives. Other authors shed light on the mechanisms that lead to the emergence of extremism [[16](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7#ref-CR16 "Meadows, M., Cliff, D.: The relative disagreement model of opinion dynamics: where do extremists come from? In: Elmenreich, W., Dressler, F., Loreto, V. (eds.) IWSOS 2013. LNCS, vol. 8221, pp. 66–77. Springer, Heidelberg (2014). 
https://doi.org/10.1007/978-3-642-54140-7_6")], particularly when extremists are introduced in the population [[6](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7#ref-CR6 "Deffuant, G., et al.: How can extremism prevail? A study based on the relative agreement interaction model. J. Artif. Soc. Soc. Simul. 5(4), 1 (2002)")]. They show, using models of “bounded-confidence”, that three different kinds of steady states (uniformity, pluriformity, bipolarization) are possible depending on whether the agents are sufficiently uncertain about their opinions and/or sufficiently connected to one another or when a significant number of them already hold an extreme opinion.  
意见传播文献中的大多数模型都对意见感兴趣，因为这些意见对集体决策和社会秩序问题有影响。例如，[ [10](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7#ref-CR10 "Galam, S., Moscovici, S.: Towards a theory of collective phenomena: consensus and attitude changes in groups. Eur. J. Soc. Psychol. 21(1), 49–74 (1991)") ]中的作者对共识的形成以及群体如何在两种选择之间进行选择感兴趣。其他作者阐明了导致极端主义出现的机制[ [16](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7#ref-CR16 "Meadows, M., Cliff, D.: The relative disagreement model of opinion dynamics: where do extremists come from? In: Elmenreich, W., Dressler, F., Loreto, V. (eds.) IWSOS 2013. LNCS, vol. 8221, pp. 66–77. Springer, Heidelberg (2014). https://doi.org/10.1007/978-3-642-54140-7_6") ]，特别是当极端分子进入人群时[ [6](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7#ref-CR6 "Deffuant, G., et al.: How can extremism prevail? A study based on the relative agreement interaction model. J. Artif. Soc. Soc. Simul. 5(4), 1 (2002)") ]。他们使用“有限置信度”模型表明，三种不同的稳态（均匀性、多态性、两极化）是可能的，这取决于代理人是否对自己的观点足够不确定和/或彼此之间有足够的联系，或者当他们中的相当一部分人已经持有极端观点。

Another stream of discrete opinion dynamics models that explain the emergence of opinions is the family of models based on Latane’s social impact theory [[19](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7#ref-CR19 "Nowak, A., Szamrej, J., Latané, B.: From private attitude to public opinion: a dynamic theory of social impact. Psychol. Rev. 97(3), 362 (1990)")]. In the theory, the agent changes opinion according to whether the informational impact she is subject to, which depends on the persuasiveness, supportiveness, and immediacy of the environment and the information she receives, is sufficiently strong. Simulations of the theory predict two emergent group phenomena: the shift of attitudes towards incompletely polarized equilibria and the formation of a coherent clustering of subgroups with deviant attitudes. Similarly, but in a continuous, more argumentative fashion, Mäs and Flache [[15](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7#ref-CR15 "Mäs, M., Flache, A.: Differentiation without distancing. Explaining bi-polarization of opinions without negative influence. PloS One 8(11), e74516 (2013)")] present a model of opinion diffusion with arguments. Arguments are considered to be for or against a proposal and given an agent-dependant relevance in dyadic persuasive interactions. They also determine the agents’ opinions and dissimilarities, as agents are assumed to infer their opinions from them. They show that opinion bipolarization can emerge from interactions among similar agents. In [[22](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7#ref-CR22 "Stefanelli, A., Seidl, R.: Moderate and polarized opinions. Using empirical data for an agent-based simulation. In: Social Simulation Conference (2014)")], a similar approach to argumentation and opinion formation is taken, but for the fact that they introduce different types of arguments, explicitly apply social judgment theory, and use survey data for model-to-real-world comparisons. Finally, in [[3](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7#ref-CR3 "Butler, G., Pigozzi, G., Rouchier, J.: Mixing dyadic and deliberative opinion dynamics in an agent-based model of group decision-making. Complexity 2019, 1–39 (2019)")] the authors study the effect of deliberation, as an argumentative process for collective decision-making, on the opinion distribution of a population. They are interested in how deliberation timing, frequency, and size in collective decision-making processes affect the evolution of opinions, the correctness of deliberated outcomes, and the coherence between what is deliberated and a hypothetical majority vote. They show that an intermediate frequency of discussions and an intermediate size of deliberation lead to consensus and to a relatively high level of correctness. Our proposition in this paper differs from [[3](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7#ref-CR3 "Butler, G., Pigozzi, G., Rouchier, J.: Mixing dyadic and deliberative opinion dynamics in an agent-based model of group decision-making. Complexity 2019, 1–39 (2019)")] in at least four key aspects: (1) an audience does not validate the final deliberated results through voting, (2) only the agents that deliberate are directly affected by deliberation, (3) agents are vigilant, and (4) they exchange arguments when they interact with one another.  
另一种解释观点出现的离散观点动态模型是基于 Latane 社会影响理论的模型系列 [ [19](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7#ref-CR19 "Nowak, A., Szamrej, J., Latané, B.: From private attitude to public opinion: a dynamic theory of social impact. Psychol. Rev. 97(3), 362 (1990)") ]。理论上，代理人根据她所受到的信息影响是否足够强来改变观点，而信息影响取决于环境和她收到的信息的说服力、支持性和即时性。该理论的模拟预测了两种新兴的群体现象：态度向不完全极化均衡的转变以及具有异常态度的子群体的连贯聚类的形成。类似地，Mäs 和 Flache [ [15](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7#ref-CR15 "Mäs, M., Flache, A.: Differentiation without distancing. Explaining bi-polarization of opinions without negative influence. PloS One 8(11), e74516 (2013)") ] 以一种连续的、更具争论性的方式提出了一种带有争论的意见传播模型。论据被认为是支持或反对某个提案，并在二元说服性互动中具有依赖于主体的相关性。它们还确定代理人的意见和差异，因为代理人被假定从他们中推断出他们的意见。他们表明，类似代理人之间的相互作用可能会出现意见两极分化。在[ [22](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7#ref-CR22 "Stefanelli, A., Seidl, R.: Moderate and polarized opinions. Using empirical data for an agent-based simulation. In: Social Simulation Conference (2014)") ]中，采用了类似的论证和意见形成方法，但事实上它们引入了不同类型的论证，明确应用社会判断理论，并使用调查数据进行模型与现实世界的比较。最后，在[ [3](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7#ref-CR3 "Butler, G., Pigozzi, G., Rouchier, J.: Mixing dyadic and deliberative opinion dynamics in an agent-based model of group decision-making. Complexity 2019, 1–39 (2019)") ]中，作者研究了商议作为集体决策的论证过程对人口意见分布的影响。 他们感兴趣的是集体决策过程中的审议时间、频率和规模如何影响意见的演变、审议结果的正确性以及审议内容与假设多数票之间的一致性。他们表明，中等频率的讨论和中等规模的审议会导致共识和相对较高的正确性。我们在本文中的主张至少在四个关键方面与[ [3](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7#ref-CR3 "Butler, G., Pigozzi, G., Rouchier, J.: Mixing dyadic and deliberative opinion dynamics in an agent-based model of group decision-making. Complexity 2019, 1–39 (2019)") ]不同：（1）受众不通过投票来验证最终的商议结果，（2）只有商议的主体才会直接受到商议的影响，（3）主体保持警惕，并且（4）他们在相互交流时交换意见。

When it comes to truth-seeking in opinion diffusion, the _funnel_ and _lead-the-pack_ theorems give sufficient conditions for truth-finding within a spectrum of opinions in continuous bounded-confidence models [[12](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7#ref-CR12 "Hegselmann, R., et al.: Truth and cognitive division of labor: first steps towards a computer aided social epistemology. J. Artif. Soc. Soc. Simul. 9(3), 10 (2006)")]. For discrete truth-seeking, authors in [[20](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7#ref-CR20 "Rouchier, J., Tanimura, E.: When overconfident agents slow down collective learning. Simulation 88(1), 33–49 (2012)")] show that learning about an exogenous correct state of the world (represented by bits) through pair-wise interactions is possible only if the agents are not too confident. In our case, correctly labeling arguments can be seen as a process of truth-seeking in which the correctness of deliberated outcomes should emerge from the system.  
当涉及意见传播中的真相寻求时，_漏斗定理_和_领先定理_为连续有限置信模型中一系列意见中的真相发现提供了充分的条件[ [12](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7#ref-CR12 "Hegselmann, R., et al.: Truth and cognitive division of labor: first steps towards a computer aided social epistemology. J. Artif. Soc. Soc. Simul. 9(3), 10 (2006)") ]。对于离散的真相寻求，[ [20](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7#ref-CR20 "Rouchier, J., Tanimura, E.: When overconfident agents slow down collective learning. Simulation 88(1), 33–49 (2012)") ]中的作者表明，只有当智能体不太自信时，才可能通过成对交互来了解世界的外生正确状态（由位表示）。在我们的例子中，正确标记论点可以被视为寻求真相的过程，其中深思熟虑的结果的正确性应该从系统中显现出来。

Back to opinion formation and abstract argumentation, Gabbriellini and Torroni [[9](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7#ref-CR9 "Gabbriellini, S., Torroni, P.: A new framework for ABMs based on argumentative reasoning. In: Kamiński, B., Koloch, G. (eds.) Advances in Social Simulation. Advances in Intelligent Systems and Computing, vol. 229, pp. 25–36. Springer, Heidelberg (2014). 
https://doi.org/10.1007/978-3-642-39829-2_3")] are the first to have originally and soundly merged opinion diffusion and abstract argumentation. They defined the agent’s opinion as a function of the arguments she holds and the attack relation among them. They devised a focused peer-to-peer dialogue system of persuasion (NetArg), inspired from Mercier and Sperber’s argumentative theory of reasoning [[17](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7#ref-CR17 "Mercier, H., Sperber, D.: Why do humans reason? Arguments for an argumentative theory. Behav. Brain Sci. 34(2), 57–74 (2011)")], that used only abstract argumentation to study opinion polarization. Moreover, they used social networks and epistemic vigilance to define a dynamics for knowledge revision and trust, which we lack in our model. They showed that if a conservative belief operator in argumentation was applied by the agents when reasoning, then their dialogue protocol did not increase polarization. They also used the model to study the effect of network structure in the spreading of arguments, but were not particularly interested in notions such as the correctness of deliberated outcomes nor in tackling questions related to deliberation procedures and multi-level opinion dynamics like we are. That being said, their system is very expressive and helps position our work at the frontier between pure argumentative opinion diffusion models, opinion diffusion with arguments, and continuous bounded-confidence models of opinion diffusion. Apart from their work, we are unaware of existing literature on agent-based modeling that explicitly relates deliberative opinion dynamics and opinion diffusion through abstract argumentation as we have done it. This is why we see our model as a contribution to the social influence and opinion dynamics fields in ABM and as a pragmatic application of abstract argumentation theory.  
回到观点形成和抽象论证，Gabbriellini 和 Torroni [ [9](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7#ref-CR9 "Gabbriellini, S., Torroni, P.: A new framework for ABMs based on argumentative reasoning. In: Kamiński, B., Koloch, G. (eds.) Advances in Social Simulation. Advances in Intelligent Systems and Computing, vol. 229, pp. 25–36. Springer, Heidelberg (2014). https://doi.org/10.1007/978-3-642-39829-2_3") ] 是第一个将观点传播和抽象论证原始而完美地融合在一起的人。他们将代理人的观点定义为她所持有的论点以及这些论点之间的攻击关系的函数。他们设计了一种集中的点对点说服对话系统（NetArg），其灵感来自 Mercier 和 Sperber 的论证推理理论 [ [17](https://link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-3-030-60843-9_7#ref-CR17 "Mercier, H., Sperber, D.: Why do humans reason? Arguments for an argumentative theory. Behav. Brain Sci. 34(2), 57–74 (2011)") ]，该系统仅使用抽象论证来研究观点极化。此外，他们利用社交网络和认知警惕来定义知识修正和信任的动态，这是我们的模型中所缺乏的。他们表明，如果智能体在推理时应用论证中的保守信念算子，那么他们的对话协议不会增加极化。他们还使用该模型来研究网络结构在争论传播中的影响，但对诸如商议结果的正确性之类的概念并不特别感兴趣，也不像我们一样对解决与商议程序和多层次意见动态相关的问题特别感兴趣。话虽这么说，他们的系统非常具有表现力，有助于将我们的工作定位在纯争论性意见传播模型、带论证的意见传播和连续有限置信的意见传播模型之间的前沿。除了他们的工作之外，我们不知道有关基于主体的建模的现有文献，正如我们所做的那样，通过抽象论证明确地将审议意见动态和意见传播联系起来。这就是为什么我们将我们的模型视为对 ABM 中社会影响力和舆论动态领域的贡献，以及抽象论证理论的务实应用。


# # A Formal Theory of Democratic Deliberation
https://www.cambridge.org/core/journals/american-political-science-review/article/formal-theory-of-democratic-deliberation/78A6828E834595C799DB4103C1C7976B?utm_source=chatgpt.com
